```python
import sys
from itertools import combinations

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if data.startswith('[') and data.endswith(']'):
    data = data[1:-1]
dice_str = [x.strip() for x in data.split(',')]
dice = [int(x) for x in dice_str if x]
counts = [0] * 6
for d in dice:
    if 1 <= d <= 6:
        counts[d - 1] += 1

three_scores = [0, 1000, 200, 300, 400, 500, 600]
memo = {}

def max_score(counts):
    if counts in memo:
        return memo[counts]
    ans = 0
    # straight
    if all(c >= 1 for c in counts):
        new_cnt = tuple(c - 1 for c in counts)
        ans = max(ans, 1000 + max_score(new_cnt))
    # three pairs
    for comb in combinations(range(6), 3):
        if all(counts[i] >= 2 for i in comb):
            new_cnt = list(counts)
            for i in comb:
                new_cnt[i] -= 2
            newt = tuple(new_cnt)
            ans = max(ans, 750 + max_score(newt))
    # k-of-a-kind
    for i in range(6):
        k = counts[i]
        if k >= 3:
            score = (k - 2) * three_scores[i + 1]
            new_cnt = list(counts)
            new_cnt[i] = 0
            newt = tuple(new_cnt)
            ans = max(ans, score + max_score(newt))
    # singles 1 (i=0) and 5 (i=4)
    for i, sc in [(0, 100), (4, 50)]:
        if counts[i] >= 1:
            new_cnt = list(counts)
            new_cnt[i] -= 1
            newt = tuple(new_cnt)
            ans = max(ans, sc + max_score(newt))
    memo[counts] = ans
    return ans

res = max_score(tuple(counts))
if res == 0:
    print("Zonk")
else:
    print(res)
```
```python
import sys
from itertools import combinations

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if data.startswith('[') and data.endswith(']'):
    data = data[1:-1]
dice_str = [x.strip() for x in data.split(',')]
dice = [int(x) for x in dice_str if x]
counts = [0] * 6
for d in dice:
    if 1 <= d <= 6:
        counts[d - 1] += 1

three_scores = [0, 1000, 200, 300, 400, 500, 600]
memo = {}

def max_score(counts):
    counts = tuple(counts)
    if counts in memo:
        return memo[counts]
    ans = 0
    # straight
    if all(c >= 1 for c in counts):
        new_cnt = tuple(c - 1 for c in counts)
        ans = max(ans, 1000 + max_score(new_cnt))
    # three pairs
    for comb in combinations(range(6), 3):
        if all(counts[i] >= 2 for i in comb):
            new_cnt = list(counts)
            for i in comb:
                new_cnt[i] -= 2
            newt = tuple(new_cnt)
            ans = max(ans, 750 + max_score(newt))
    # k-of-a-kind
    for i in range(6):
        k = counts[i]
        if k >= 3:
            score = (k - 2) * three_scores[i + 1]
            new_cnt = list(counts)
            new_cnt[i] = 0
            newt = tuple(new_cnt)
            ans = max(ans, score + max_score(newt))
    # singles 1 (i=0) and 5 (i=4)
    for i, sc in [(0, 100), (4, 50)]:
        if counts[i] >= 1:
            new_cnt = list(counts)
            new_cnt[i] -= 1
            newt = tuple(new_cnt)
            ans = max(ans, sc + max_score(newt))
    memo[counts] = ans
    return ans

res = max_score(counts)
if res == 0:
    print("Zonk")
else:
    print(res)

```python
def drop_cap(s):
    result = []
    i = 0
    n = len(s)
    while i < n:
        if s[i].isspace():
            result.append(s[i])
            i += 1
        else:
            start = i
            while i < n and not s[i].isspace():
                i += 1
            word = s[start:i]
            word_len = len(word)
            if word_len > 2:
                first = word[0].upper()
                rest = ''.join(c.lower() for c in word[1:])
                result.append(first + rest)
            else:
                result.append(word)
    return ''.join(result)

s = input()
print(drop_cap(s))

import sys

def possibles(c):
    if c == 'a':
        return {'b'}
    if c == 'z':
        return {'y'}
    return {chr(ord(c) - 1), chr(ord(c) + 1)}

s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(s)
is_possible = True
for i in range((n + 1) // 2):
    A = possibles(s[i])
    B = possibles(s[n - 1 - i])
    if not (A & B):
        is_possible = False
        break
print(is_possible)

```python
s = input().strip()
n = len(s)
parts = []
for i in range(n):
    digit = int(s[i])
    if digit != 0:
        power = n - 1 - i
        term = str(digit)
        if power > 0:
            pow10 = '1' + '0' * power
            term += '*' + pow10
        parts.append(term)
output = '+'.join(parts)
print(output)

completed 4/150, Solved: True, number of success = 1/4, acc = 25.0
```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().splitlines()
s1 = data[0]
s2 = data[1]

mapping = {}
used = set()
possible = True

for i in range(len(s1)):
    c1 = s1[i]
    c2 = s2[i]
    if c1 in mapping:
        if mapping[c1] != c2:
            possible = False
            break
    else:
        if c2 in used:
            possible = False
            break
        mapping[c1] = c2
        used.add(c2)

print("True" if possible else "False")

completed 5/150, Solved: False, number of success = 1/5, acc = 20.0
```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)

if n == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
first_l = -1
last_r = -1
for i in range(n):
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)
    if s[i] == '[' and first_l == -1:
        first_l = i
    if s[i] == ']':
        last_r = i

if first_l == -1 or last_r == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

min_so_far = float('inf')
max_len = -1
for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == ':' and i > first_l:
        # Try as c
        if i < last_r and min_so_far != float('inf'):
            pipes = prefix[i] - min_so_far
            max_len = max(max_len, 4 + pipes)
        # Add as potential b
        this_val = prefix[i + 1]
        min_so_far = min(min_so_far, this_val)

print(max_len if max_len != -1 else -1)
```
```python
def super_size(n_str):
    digits = list(n_str)
    digits.sort(reverse=True)
    return ''.join(digits)

num = input().strip()
print(super_size(num))

```python
def elevator(left, right, call):
    dist_l = abs(left - call)
    dist_r = abs(right - call)
    if dist_l < dist_r:
        return "left"
    else:
        return "right"

left = int(input().strip())
right = int(input().strip())
call = int(input().strip())
print(elevator(left, right, call))
```

completed 9/150, Solved: False, number of success = 2/9, acc = 22.22
```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)

if n == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

pipe_prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe_prefix[i + 1] = pipe_prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

has_left = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    has_left[i + 1] = has_left[i] or (s[i] == '[')

has_right = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    has_right[i] = (s[i] == ']') or has_right[i + 1]

colons = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']
m = len(colons)

INF = 10**9 + 7
current_min = INF
max_m = -1

for r in range(m):
    cq = colons[r]
    if has_right[cq + 1] and current_min < INF:
        this_m = pipe_prefix[cq] - current_min
        if this_m > max_m:
            max_m = this_m
    if has_left[cq]:
        current_min = min(current_min, pipe_prefix[cq + 1])

if max_m == -1:
    print(-1)
else:
    print(4 + max_m)

completed 10/150, Solved: False, number of success = 2/10, acc = 20.0
```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

prefix_open = [0] * (n + 1)
prefix_pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_open[i + 1] = prefix_open[i] + (1 if s[i] == '[' else 0)
    prefix_pipe[i + 1] = prefix_pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

suffix_close = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    suffix_close[i] = suffix_close[i + 1] + (1 if s[i] == ']' else 0)

min_prefix = float('inf')
max_count = -1
for k in range(n):
    if s[k] == ':':
        # Try as right colon
        if suffix_close[k + 1] >= 1 and min_prefix != float('inf'):
            count = prefix_pipe[k] - min_prefix
            if count > max_count:
                max_count = count
        # Try as left colon
        if prefix_open[k] >= 1:
            min_prefix = min(min_prefix, prefix_pipe[k + 1])

if max_count >= 0:
    print(4 + max_count)
else:
    print(-1)
```

q[1] = 1
q[2] = 1
for i in range(3, n + 1):

```python
import sys
import ast

def anagrams(word, wordlist):
    if not word:
        return []
    sorted_word = ''.join(sorted(word))
    result = []
    for w in wordlist:
        if len(w) == len(word) and ''.join(sorted(w)) == sorted_word:
            result.append(w)
    return result

# Read input
data = sys.stdin.read().strip().split('\n')
word = data[0].strip()
wordlist_str = data[1].strip() if len(data) > 1 else '[]'

# Parse wordlist using ast.literal_eval safely
wordlist = ast.literal_eval(wordlist_str)

# Get result
result = anagrams(word, wordlist)

# Print as list string
print(str(result))
```
```python
import sys
import ast

def anagrams(word, wordlist):
    if not word:
        return []
    sorted_word = ''.join(sorted(word))
    result = []
    for w in wordlist:
        if len(w) == len(word) and ''.join(sorted(w)) == sorted_word:
            result.append(w)
    return result

# Read input
data = sys.stdin.read().strip().split('\n')
word = data[0].strip()
wordlist_str = data[1].strip() if len(data) > 1 else '[]'

# Parse wordlist using ast.literal_eval safely
wordlist = ast.literal_eval(wordlist_str)

# Get result
result = anagrams(word, wordlist)

# Print as list string
print(str(result))

completed 12/150, Solved: False, number of success = 2/12, acc = 16.67
```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

# Compute left_open[i]: exists '[' before i
left_open = [False] * n
has_lo = False
for i in range(n):
    left_open[i] = has_lo
    if s[i] == '[':
        has_lo = True

# Compute right_close[i]: exists ']' after i
right_close = [False] * n
has_rc = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    right_close[i] = has_rc
    if s[i] == ']':
        has_rc = True

# Compute pipe_prefix[i+1] = number of '|' in 0..i
pipe_prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe_prefix[i + 1] = pipe_prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

# Find max length
INF = sys.maxsize
min_pref = INF
max_len = -1

for i in range(n):
    # Check if i can be p2 (second colon)
    if s[i] == ':' and right_close[i]:
        if min_pref != INF:
            cnt = pipe_prefix[i] - min_pref
            max_len = max(max_len, 4 + cnt)
    # Add i as possible p1 (first colon) for future p2
    if s[i] == ':' and left_open[i]:
        min_pref = min(min_pref, pipe_prefix[i + 1])

print(max_len if max_len != -1 else -1)

import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

# Compute left_open[i]: exists '[' before i
left_open = [False] * n
has_lo = False
for i in range(n):
    left_open[i] = has_lo
    if s[i] == '[':
        has_lo = True

# Compute right_close[i]: exists ']' after i
right_close = [False] * n
has_rc = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    right_close[i] = has_rc
    if s[i] == ']':
        has_rc = True

# Compute pipe_prefix[i+1] = number of '|' in 0..i
pipe_prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe_prefix[i + 1] = pipe_prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

max_len = -1

completed 13/150, Solved: False, number of success = 2/13, acc = 15.38
```python
import sys

def main():
    s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
    n = len(s)
    if n == 0:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Find first_open
    first_open = n
    for i in range(n):
        if s[i] == '[':
            first_open = i
            break

    # Find last_close
    last_close = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        if s[i] == ']':
            last_close = i
            break

    if first_open == n or last_close == -1:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Compute prefix for |
    pref = [0] * (n + 1)
    for i in range(n):
        pref[i + 1] = pref[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

    # Collect colon positions
    cols = []
    for i in range(n):
        if s[i] == ':':
            cols.append(i)
    m = len(cols)
    if m < 2:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Find j_start: first colon with pos > first_open
    j_start = 0
    while j_start < m and cols[j_start] <= first_open:
        j_start += 1
    if j_start >= m or j_start + 1 >= m:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Now compute max pipes
    min_so_far = pref[cols[j_start] + 1]
    max_num_pipes = -1
    for k in range(j_start + 1, m):
        i3_pos = cols[k]
        if i3_pos < last_close:
            cand = pref[i3_pos] - min_so_far
            if cand > max_num_pipes:
                max_num_pipes = cand
        # Update min_so_far with this k's v
        min_so_far = min(min_so_far, pref[cols[k] + 1])

    if max_num_pipes == -1:
        print(-1)
    else:
        print(4 + max_num_pipes)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```
```python
import sys

def main():
    s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
    n = len(s)
    if n == 0:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Find first_open
    first_open = n
    for i in range(n):
        if s[i] == '[':
            first_open = i
            break

    # Find last_close
    last_close = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        if s[i] == ']':
            last_close = i
            break

    if first_open == n or last_close == -1:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Compute prefix for |
    pref = [0] * (n + 1)
    for i in range(n):
        pref[i + 1] = pref[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

    # Collect colon positions
    cols = []
    for i in range(n):
        if s[i] == ':':
            cols.append(i)
    m = len(cols)
    if m < 2:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Find j_start: first colon with pos > first_open
    j_start = 0
    while j_start < m and cols[j_start] <= first_open:
        j_start += 1
    if j_start >= m or j_start + 1 >= m:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Now compute max pipes
    min_so_far = pref[cols[j_start] + 1]
    max_num_pipes = -1
    for k in range(j_start + 1, m):
        i3_pos = cols[k]
        if i3_pos < last_close:
            cand = pref[i3_pos] - min_so_far
            if cand > max_num_pipes:
                max_num_pipes = cand
        # Update min_so_far with this k's v
        min_so_far = min(min_so_far, pref[cols[k] + 1])

    if max_num_pipes == -1:
        print(-1)
    else:
        print(4 + max_num_pipes)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```python
def nameInStr(str, name):
    str = str.lower()
    name = name.lower()
    i = 0
    j = 0
    while i < len(str) and j < len(name):
        if str[i] == name[j]:
            j += 1
        i += 1
    return j == len(name)

s = input()
n = input()
print(nameInStr(s, n))

completed 16/150, Solved: True, number of success = 3/16, acc = 18.75
```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

# Compute left_open[i]: True if there is '[' in [0..i-1]
left_open = [False] * (n + 1)
count_open = 0
for i in range(n):
    left_open[i] = count_open > 0
    if s[i] == '[':
        count_open += 1
left_open[n] = count_open > 0

# Compute right_close[i]: True if there is ']' in [i..n-1]
right_close = [False] * (n + 1)
count_close = 0
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    if s[i] == ']':
        count_close += 1
    right_close[i] = count_close > 0
right_close[n] = False

# Compute pipe_prefix[i+1] = number of '|' in [0..i]
pipe_prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe_prefix[i + 1] = pipe_prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

# Collect colon positions
colon_pos = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']
m = len(colon_pos)
if m < 2:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Now iterate over possible q
min_prefix = float('inf')
max_pipes = -1  # since 0 is possible, use -1 as invalid

for q in range(m):
    cq = colon_pos[q]
    if right_close[cq + 1] and min_prefix != float('inf'):
        pipes = pipe_prefix[cq] - min_prefix
        if pipes > max_pipes:
            max_pipes = pipes
    # Add this as potential p for future q
    if left_open[cq]:
        this_prefix = pipe_prefix[cq + 1]
        if this_prefix < min_prefix:
            min_prefix = this_prefix

if max_pipes == -1:
    print(-1)
else:
    print(4 + max_pipes)

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

# Compute left_open[i]: True if there is '[' in [0..i-1]
left_open = [False] * (n + 1)
count_open = 0
for i in range(n):
    left_open[i] = count_open > 0
    if s[i] == '[':
        count_open += 1
left_open[n] = count_open > 0

# Compute right_close[i]: True if there is ']' in [i..n-1]
right_close = [False] * (n + 1)
count_close = 0
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    if s[i] == ']':
        count_close += 1
    right_close[i] = count_close > 0
right_close[n] = False

# Compute pipe_prefix[i+1] = number of '|' in [0..i]
pipe_prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe_prefix[i + 1] = pipe_prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

# Collect colon positions
colon_pos = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']
m = len(colon_pos)
if m < 2:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Now iterate over possible q
min_prefix = float('inf')
max_pipes = -1  # since 0 is possible, use -1 as invalid

for q in range(m):
    cq = colon_pos[q]
    if right_close[cq + 1] and min_prefix != float('inf'):
        pipes = pipe_prefix[cq] - min_prefix
        if pipes > max_pipes:
            max_pipes = pipes
    # Add this as potential p for future q
    if left_open[cq]:
        this_prefix = pipe_prefix[cq + 1]
        if this_prefix < min_prefix:
            min_prefix = this_prefix

if max_pipes == -1:
    print(-1)
else:
    print(4 + max_pipes)

```python
def getAllPrimeFactors(n):
    if n <= 0:
        return []
    if n == 1:
        return [1]
    factors = []
    while n % 2 == 0:
        factors.append(2)
        n //= 2
    i = 3
    while i * i <= n:
        while n % i == 0:
            factors.append(i)
            n //= i
        i += 2
    if n > 1:
        factors.append(n)
    return factors

def getUniquePrimeFactorsWithCount(n):
    if n <= 0:
        return [[], []]
    if n == 1:
        return [[1], [1]]
    primes = []
    counts = []
    temp_n = n
    count = 0
    while temp_n % 2 == 0:
        count += 1
        temp_n //= 2
    if count > 0:
        primes.append(2)
        counts.append(count)
    i = 3
    while i * i <= temp_n:
        count = 0
        while temp_n % i == 0:
            count += 1
            temp_n //= i
        if count > 0:
            primes.append(i)
            counts.append(count)
        i += 2
    if temp_n > 1:
        primes.append(temp_n)
        counts.append(1)
    return [primes, counts]

def getUniquePrimeFactorsWithProducts(n):
    if n <= 0:
        return []
    if n == 1:
        return [1]
    prods = []
    temp_n = n
    count = 0
    while temp_n % 2 == 0:
        count += 1
        temp_n //= 2
    if count > 0:
        prods.append(2 ** count)
    i = 3
    while i * i <= temp_n:
        count = 0
        while temp_n % i == 0:
            count += 1
            temp_n //= i
        if count > 0:
            prods.append(i ** count)
        i += 2
    if temp_n > 1:
        prods.append(temp_n)
    return prods

try:
    n = int(input().strip())
    result = getAllPrimeFactors(n)
except ValueError:
    result = []
print('[' + ', '.join(map(str, result)) + ']')

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()

n = len(data)
s = data

pipe_prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe_prefix[i + 1] = pipe_prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

prefix_has_open = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_has_open[i + 1] = prefix_has_open[i] or (s[i] == '[')

suffix_has_close = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    suffix_has_close[i] = suffix_has_close[i + 1] or (s[i] == ']')

min_prefix_left = float('inf')
has_left = False
max_pipes = -1

for j in range(n):
    if s[j] == ':':
        # Try as right colon
        if j + 1 <= n and suffix_has_close[j + 1] and has_left:
            pipes = pipe_prefix[j] - min_prefix_left
            if pipes > max_pipes:
                max_pipes = pipes
        # Add as left candidate if possible
        if prefix_has_open[j]:
            new_pref = pipe_prefix[j + 1]
            if new_pref < min_prefix_left:
                min_prefix_left = new_pref
            has_left = True

if max_pipes >= 0:
    print(4 + max_pipes)
else:
    print(-1)

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)
max_len = 0
best_start = -1
best_end = -1

for i in range(n - 1):
    if (s[i] == '!' or s[i] == '?') and (s[i + 1] == '!' or s[i + 1] == '?') and s[i] != s[i + 1]:
        A = s[i]
        start = i
        while start >= 0 and s[start] == A:
            start -= 1
        start += 1
        L = i - start + 1

        B = s[i + 1]
        end = i + 1
        while end < n and s[end] == B:
            end += 1
        R = end - (i + 1)
        total = L + R

        if total > max_len:
            max_len = total
            best_start = start
            best_end = end
        elif total == max_len:
            if start < best_start:
                best_start = start
                best_end = end

if max_len >= 2:
    print(s[best_start:best_end])
else:
    print("")

completed 20/150, Solved: True, number of success = 4/20, acc = 20.0
```python
import sys
import ast

# Read the entire input
data = sys.stdin.read().strip()

# Safely evaluate the input as a Python list
couples = ast.literal_eval(data)

# Initialize variables to track the maximum difference and the corresponding couple
max_diff = -1
best = None

# Iterate through each couple
for couple in couples:
    # Split the couple by '-'
    parts = couple.split('-')
    # Assume valid input with exactly two parts
    a = int(parts[0])
    b = int(parts[1])
    # Calculate absolute difference
    d = abs(a - b)
    # Update if this difference is strictly greater than the current max
    # This ensures we pick the first one in case of ties
    if d > max_diff:
        max_diff = d
        best = couple

# Output the result
if max_diff > 0:
    print(best)
else:
    print("false")
```

## Let's think step by step.

1. Import necessary modules: `sys` for reading input and `ast` for safely parsing the list literal.
2. Read the entire standard input and strip whitespace to get the list string, e.g., `['56-23','1-100']`.
3. Use `ast.literal_eval` to parse the string into a Python list of strings.
4. Initialize `max_diff = -1` and `best = None` to track the maximum difference found and the corresponding couple string.
5. Iterate through each couple in the order given:
   - Split the string by `'-'` to get the two numbers.
   - Convert them to integers using `int()`.
   - Compute the absolute difference `d = abs(a - b)`.
   - If `d > max_diff`, update `max_diff = d` and `best = couple`. (Strictly greater ensures the first couple is kept in case of ties.)
6. After processing all couples, check if `max_diff > 0`:
   - If yes, print the `best` couple string.
   - If no (all differences are 0 or list is empty), print `"false"`.
7. This handles all cases: maximum difference selection, ties by position, and zero-difference scenarios correctly. No leading zeros issue since we output the original strings.
```python
import sys
import ast

# Read the entire input
data = sys.stdin.read().strip()

# Safely evaluate the input as a Python list
couples = ast.literal_eval(data)

# Initialize variables to track the maximum difference and the corresponding couple
max_diff = -1
best = None

# Iterate through each couple
for couple in couples:
    # Split the couple by '-'
    parts = couple.split('-')
    # Assume valid input with exactly two parts
    a = int(parts[0])
    b = int(parts[1])
    # Calculate absolute difference
    d = abs(a - b)
    # Update if this difference is strictly greater than the current max
    # This ensures we pick the first one in case of ties
    if d > max_diff:
        max_diff = d
        best = couple

# Output the result
if max_diff > 0:
    print(best)
else:
    print("false")

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)

# Prefix sum for '|'
prefix_pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_pipe[i + 1] = prefix_pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

# has_open_prefix[i]: exists '[' in [0..i-1]
has_open_prefix = [False] * n
seen_open = False
for i in range(n):
    has_open_prefix[i] = seen_open
    if s[i] == '[':
        seen_open = True

# has_close_suffix[i]: exists ']' in [i+1..n-1]
has_close_suffix = [False] * n
seen_close = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    has_close_suffix[i] = seen_close
    if s[i] == ']':
        seen_close = True

# Now scan
min_after = float('inf')
max_len = -1
for k in range(n):
    # First check if can be second ':'
    if s[k] == ':' and has_close_suffix[k]:
        if min_after != float('inf'):
            count = prefix_pipe[k] - min_after
            max_len = max(max_len, 4 + count)
    # Then update if can be first ':'
    if s[k] == ':' and has_open_prefix[k]:
        min_after = min(min_after, prefix_pipe[k + 1])

print(max_len if max_len != -1 else -1)

completed 22/150, Solved: False, number of success = 4/22, acc = 18.18
```python
def process_token(token):
    n = len(token)
    last_alpha = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        if token[i].isalpha():
            last_alpha = i
            break
    if last_alpha == -1:
        return token
    body = token[:last_alpha + 1]
    trailing = token[last_alpha + 1:]
    len_b = len(body)
    count_t = sum(1 for c in body if c.lower() == 't')
    if len_b > 6 or count_t >= 2:
        new_body = body[::-1]
    elif len_b == 1:
        new_body = '0'
    elif len_b == 2 or trailing.startswith(','):
        new_body = body.upper()
    else:
        new_body = body
    return new_body + trailing

s = input()
result = []
i = 0
n = len(s)
while i < n:
    if s[i].isspace():
        result.append(s[i])
        i += 1
        continue
    j = i
    while j < n and not s[j].isspace():
        j += 1
    token = s[i:j]
    new_token = process_token(token)
    result.append(new_token)
    i = j
print(''.join(result), end='')
```
```python
def process_token(token):
    n = len(token)
    last_alpha = -1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        if token[i].isalpha():
            last_alpha = i
            break
    if last_alpha == -1:
        return token
    body = token[:last_alpha + 1]
    trailing = token[last_alpha + 1:]
    len_b = len(body)
    count_t = sum(1 for c in body if c.lower() == 't')
    if len_b > 6 or count_t >= 2:
        new_body = body[::-1]
    elif len_b == 2 or trailing.startswith(','):
        new_body = body.upper()
    elif len_b == 1:
        new_body = '0'
    else:
        new_body = body
    return new_body + trailing

s = input()
result = []
i = 0
n = len(s)
while i < n:
    if s[i].isspace():
        result.append(s[i])
        i += 1
        continue
    j = i
    while j < n and not s[j].isspace():
        j += 1
    token = s[i:j]
    new_token = process_token(token)
    result.append(new_token)
    i = j
print(''.join(result), end='')

```python
import sys

s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(s)

prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

colon_pos = []
has_left = []
seen_open = False
for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == '[':
        seen_open = True
    if s[i] == ':':
        colon_pos.append(i)
        has_left.append(seen_open)

m = len(colon_pos)
if m < 2:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

has_right = [False] * m
seen_close = False
j = m - 1
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    if s[i] == ']':
        seen_close = True
    if j >= 0 and i == colon_pos[j]:
        has_right[j] = seen_close
        j -= 1

min_prefix_left = n + 1
max_acc = -1
for bb in range(m):
    if has_right[bb] and min_prefix_left <= n:
        count = prefix[colon_pos[bb]] - min_prefix_left
        max_acc = max(max_acc, 4 + count)
    if has_left[bb]:
        this_p = prefix[colon_pos[bb] + 1]
        if this_p < min_prefix_left:
            min_prefix_left = this_p

print(max_acc if max_acc != -1 else -1)

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)

if n <= 1:
    print("false")
else:
    cum_open = [0] * (n + 1)
    cum_close = [0] * (n + 1)
    for i in range(n):
        cum_open[i + 1] = cum_open[i] + (1 if s[i] == '[' else 0)
        cum_close[i + 1] = cum_close[i] + (1 if s[i] == ']' else 0)
    valid = True
    for i in range(n + 1):
        if cum_open[i] < cum_close[i]:
            valid = False
            break
    if cum_open[n] != cum_close[n]:
        valid = False
    print("true" if valid else "false")

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

# Find leftmost '['
left_open = n
for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == '[':
        left_open = i
        break

# Find rightmost ']'
right_close = -1
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    if s[i] == ']':
        right_close = i
        break

if left_open == n or right_close == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

start_p = left_open + 1
end_q = right_close - 1

if start_p > end_q:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Prefix sum for '|'
pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe[i + 1] = pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

# Collect valid colon positions
pos = []
for i in range(start_p, end_q + 1):
    if s[i] == ':':
        pos.append(i)

m = len(pos)
if m < 2:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find max number of '|' between two colons
INF = 10**9
min_after = INF
max_cnt = -1
for l in range(m):
    q = pos[l]
    if min_after < INF:
        cnt = pipe[q] - min_after
        if cnt > max_cnt:
            max_cnt = cnt
    # Update for this as potential p
    p1 = pos[l] + 1
    min_after = min(min_after, pipe[p1])

print(4 + max_cnt)

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()

# Remove outer brackets
if data.startswith('[') and data.endswith(']'):
    data = data[1:-1]

# Split by comma and strip spaces, convert to int
nums_str = data.split(',')
nums = []
for x in nums_str:
    nums.append(int(x.strip()))

# Filter elements where nums[i] % i == 0 for i > 0
result = []
for i in range(len(nums)):
    if i > 0 and nums[i] % i == 0:
        result.append(nums[i])

# Format output
output = '[' + ', '.join(map(str, result)) + ']'
print(output)

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()

# Remove outer brackets
if data.startswith('[') and data.endswith(']'):
    data = data[1:-1]

# Split by comma and strip spaces, convert to int
nums_str = data.split(',')
nums = []
for x in nums_str:
    nums.append(int(x.strip()))

# Filter elements where nums[i] % i == 0 for i > 0
result = []
for i in range(len(nums)):
    if i > 0 and nums[i] % i == 0:
        result.append(nums[i])

# Format output
output = '[' + ', '.join(map(str, result)) + ']'
print(output)

```python
s = input().strip()
lower_s = s.lower()
yellow_to_green = {
    "gold": "ForestGreen",
    "khaki": "LimeGreen",
    "lemonchiffon": "PaleGreen",
    "lightgoldenrodyellow": "SpringGreen",
    "lightyellow": "MintCream",
    "palegoldenrod": "LightGreen",
    "yellow": "Lime"
}
if lower_s in yellow_to_green:
    print(yellow_to_green[lower_s])
else:
    if len(s) == 7 and s.startswith('#') and all(c in '0123456789abcdefABCDEF' for c in s[1:]):
        r = int(s[1:3], 16)
        g = int(s[3:5], 16)
        b = int(s[5:7], 16)
        if r > b and g > b:
            vals = sorted([r, g, b])
            new_r = vals[0]
            new_g = vals[2]
            new_b = vals[1]
            hex_part_orig = s[1:]
            has_upper = any(c.isupper() for c in hex_part_orig)
            r_hex = f"{new_r:02x}"
            g_hex = f"{new_g:02x}"
            b_hex = f"{new_b:02x}"
            new_hex_part = r_hex + g_hex + b_hex
            if has_upper:
                new_hex_part = new_hex_part.upper()
            print('#' + new_hex_part)
        else:
            print(s)
    else:
        print(s)

completed 31/150, Solved: True, number of success = 7/31, acc = 22.58
```python
import sys

def main():
    input = sys.stdin.read
    data = input().split()
    a = int(data[0])
    b = int(data[1])

    N = 500001
    is_prime = [True] * N
    is_prime[0] = is_prime[1] = False
    for i in range(2, int(N**0.5) + 1):
        if is_prime[i]:
            for j in range(i*i, N, i):
                is_prime[j] = False

    primes = [i for i in range(N) if is_prime[i]]

    sum_dom = 0
    for pos in range(1, len(primes) + 1):
        p = primes[pos - 1]
        if p > b:
            break
        if is_prime[pos] and a <= p <= b:
            sum_dom += p

    print(sum_dom)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```
```python
import sys

def main():
    input = sys.stdin.read
    data = input().split()
    a = int(data[0])
    b = int(data[1])

    N = 500001
    is_prime = [True] * N
    is_prime[0] = is_prime[1] = False
    for i in range(2, int(N**0.5) + 1):
        if is_prime[i]:
            for j in range(i*i, N, i):
                is_prime[j] = False

    primes = [i for i in range(N) if is_prime[i]]

    sum_dom = 0
    for pos in range(1, len(primes) + 1):
        p = primes[pos - 1]
        if p > b:
            break
        if is_prime[pos] and a <= p <= b:
            sum_dom += p

    print(sum_dom)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```python
def tiyFizzBuzz(s):
    vowels = set('aeiouAEIOU')
    result = []
    for char in s:
        if char.isalpha():
            if char.isupper():
                if char in vowels:
                    result.append("Iron Yard")
                else:
                    result.append("Iron")
            else:  # lowercase
                if char in vowels:
                    result.append("Yard")
                else:
                    result.append(char)
        else:
            result.append(char)
    return ''.join(result)

# Read input from standard input
s = input()
# Call the function and print the output
print(tiyFizzBuzz(s))
```

def tiyFizzBuzz(s):

    result = []
    for char in s:

            if char.isupper():
                if char in vowels:
                    result.append("Iron Yard")

                    result.append("Iron")
            else:  # lowercase
                if char in vowels:
                    result.append("Yard")

                    result.append(char)

```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(NULL);
    string s;
    cin >> s;
    int n = s.size();
    vector<long long> prefix_open(n + 1, 0);
    vector<long long> prefix_pipe(n + 1, 0);
    for (int i = 1; i <= n; ++i) {
        prefix_open[i] = prefix_open[i - 1] + (s[i - 1] == '[');
        prefix_pipe[i] = prefix_pipe[i - 1] + (s[i - 1] == '|');
    }
    vector<long long> suffix_close(n + 1, 0);
    for (int i = n - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
        suffix_close[i] = suffix_close[i + 1] + (s[i] == ']');
    }
    vector<int> cols;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i) {
        if (s[i] == ':') {
            cols.push_back(i);
        }
    }
    long long min_prev_pipe = LLONG_MAX / 2;
    long long max_pipes = -1;
    for (size_t idx = 0; idx < cols.size(); ++idx) {
        int ct = cols[idx];
        if (ct + 1 <= n && suffix_close[ct + 1] >= 1 && min_prev_pipe < LLONG_MAX / 2) {
            long long pipes = prefix_pipe[ct] - min_prev_pipe;
            if (pipes > max_pipes) {
                max_pipes = pipes;
            }
        }
        if (prefix_open[ct] >= 1) {
            long long this_pipe = prefix_pipe[ct];
            if (this_pipe < min_prev_pipe) {
                min_prev_pipe = this_pipe;
            }
        }
    }
    if (max_pipes == -1) {
        cout << -1 << endl;
    } else {
        cout << 4 + max_pipes << endl;
    }
    return 0;
}
```

```python
import sys

def can_make(sequence):
    n = len(sequence)
    def check(skip):
        prev = None
        for j in range(n):
            if j == skip:
                continue
            curr = sequence[j]
            if prev is not None and prev >= curr:
                return False
            prev = curr
        return True
    if check(-1):
        return True
    for i in range(n):
        if check(i):
            return True
    return False

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if data.startswith('[') and data.endswith(']'):
    arr_str = data[1:-1].split(',')
    sequence = [int(x.strip()) for x in arr_str if x.strip()]
else:
    sequence = []
print(can_make(sequence))

completed 35/150, Solved: False, number of success = 8/35, acc = 22.86
```python
import sys
import bisect

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

first_open = n
last_close = -1
colons = []
for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == '[':
        first_open = min(first_open, i)
    elif s[i] == ']':
        last_close = max(last_close, i)
    elif s[i] == ':':
        colons.append(i)

prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

m = len(colons)
if m < 2 or first_open == n or last_close == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

k_start = bisect.bisect_right(colons, first_open)
l_max = bisect.bisect_left(colons, last_close) - 1

if k_start > l_max:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

min_sub = 10**9
max_pipes = -1
for j in range(m):
    pos = colons[j]
    # Try as second colon
    if pos < last_close:
        if j > k_start and min_sub < 10**9 // 2:
            pipes = prefix[pos] - min_sub
            if pipes > max_pipes:
                max_pipes = pipes
    # Update as potential first colon
    if pos > first_open:
        this_sub = prefix[pos + 1]
        if this_sub < min_sub:
            min_sub = this_sub

if max_pipes >= 0:
    print(4 + max_pipes)
else:
    print(-1)

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)

# Prefix sum for '|'
prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

# any_open_left[i]: True if there is '[' before position i (in 0..i-1)
open_left = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    open_left[i] = open_left[i - 1] or (s[i - 1] == '[')

# any_close_right[i]: True if there is ']' after position i (in i+1..n-1)
close_right = [False] * n
cur = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    close_right[i] = cur
    if s[i] == ']':
        cur = True

# Positions of ':'
cols = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']

min_after = n + 1
max_pipes = -1

for pos in cols:
    # Try as second ':'
    if close_right[pos] and min_after <= n:
        pipes = prefix[pos] - min_after
        if pipes > max_pipes:
            max_pipes = pipes
    # Try as first ':'
    if open_left[pos]:
        after = prefix[pos + 1]
        if after < min_after:
            min_after = after

if max_pipes >= 0:
    print(4 + max_pipes)
else:
    print(-1)

```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(0);
    string s;
    cin >> s;
    int n = s.size();
    int first_open = n;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i) {
        if (s[i] == '[') {
            first_open = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    int last_close = -1;
    for (int i = n - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
        if (s[i] == ']') {
            last_close = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    if (first_open == n || last_close == -1 || first_open >= last_close) {
        cout << -1 << endl;
        return 0;
    }
    vector<long long> pp(n + 1, 0);
    for (int i = 1; i <= n; ++i) {
        pp[i] = pp[i - 1] + (s[i - 1] == '|' ? 1LL : 0);
    }
    int left_c = -1;
    for (int i = first_open + 1; i < last_close; ++i) {
        if (s[i] == ':') {
            left_c = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    if (left_c == -1) {
        cout << -1 << endl;
        return 0;
    }
    int right_c = -1;
    for (int i = last_close - 1; i > first_open; --i) {
        if (s[i] == ':') {
            right_c = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    if (right_c == -1 || right_c <= left_c) {
        cout << -1 << endl;
        return 0;
    }
    long long pipes = pp[right_c] - pp[left_c + 1];
    cout << 4 + pipes << endl;
    return 0;
}
```

```python
import sys

def find_missing(shuffled):
    nums = [int(x) for x in shuffled[1:-1].split(', ')]
    n = len(nums) + 1
    expected = n * (n + 1) // 2
    actual = sum(nums)
    return expected - actual

input_str = sys.stdin.read().strip()
missing = find_missing(input_str)
print(missing)

import sys

s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(s)

prefix_pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
prefix_open = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_pipe[i + 1] = prefix_pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)
    prefix_open[i + 1] = prefix_open[i] + (1 if s[i] == '[' else 0)

suffix_close = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    suffix_close[i] = (s[i] == ']') or suffix_close[i + 1]

colon_pos = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']

min_valid = float('inf')
max_k = -1
for j in colon_pos:
    # Try as second colon
    if min_valid < float('inf') and j + 1 <= n and suffix_close[j + 1]:

        if k > max_k:

    # Update as potential first colon
    if prefix_open[j] > 0:
        min_valid = min(min_valid, prefix_pipe[j + 1])

if max_k == -1:

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if data.startswith('['):
    data = data[1:]
if data.endswith(']'):
    data = data[:-1]
arr = [int(x.strip()) for x in data.split(',') if x.strip()]

n = len(arr)
max_prod = float('-inf')
best = float('inf')

for i in range(n):
    prod = 1
    for j in range(n):
        if j != i:
            prod *= arr[j]
    if prod > max_prod or (prod == max_prod and arr[i] < best):
        max_prod = prod
        best = arr[i]

print(best)

```python
from collections import deque
import sys

num = int(sys.stdin.readline().strip())

if num == 1:
    print(0)
    sys.exit(0)

q = deque()
q.append((1, 0))
visited = set([1])

while q:
    curr, steps = q.popleft()
    if curr == num:
        print(steps)
        sys.exit(0)
    
    # +1
    next1 = curr + 1
    if next1 <= num and next1 not in visited:
        visited.add(next1)
        q.append((next1, steps + 1))
    
    # *2
    next2 = curr * 2
    if next2 <= num and next2 not in visited:
        visited.add(next2)
        q.append((next2, steps + 1))
```
```python
from collections import deque
import sys

num = int(sys.stdin.readline().strip())

if num == 1:
    print(0)
    sys.exit(0)

q = deque()
q.append((1, 0))
visited = set([1])

while q:
    curr, steps = q.popleft()
    if curr == num:
        print(steps)
        sys.exit(0)
    
    # +1
    next1 = curr + 1
    if next1 <= num and next1 not in visited:
        visited.add(next1)
        q.append((next1, steps + 1))
    
    # *2
    next2 = curr * 2
    if next2 <= num and next2 not in visited:
        visited.add(next2)
        q.append((next2, steps + 1))

```python
import sys

def get_primes(n):

```python
import sys

def get_primes(n):
    if n <= 2:
        return []
    sieve = [True] * n
    sieve[0] = sieve[1] = False
    for i in range(2, int(n**0.5) + 1):
        if sieve[i]:
            for j in range(i * i, n, i):
                sieve[j] = False
    return [i for i in range(n) if sieve[i]]

input_data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
N = int(input_data)
primes = get_primes(N)
k = len(primes)
count = k * (k - 1) // 2
if k == 0:
    print("[0, 0]")
else:
    prefix = 0
    total = 0.0
    for j in range(k):
        if j > 0:
            total += prefix / primes[j]
        prefix += primes[j]
    int_part = int(total)
    print(f"[{count}, {int_part}]")

```python
import sys

def merge(arr, temp, left, mid, right):
    inv_count = 0
    i = left
    j = mid
    k = left
    while (i <= mid - 1) and (j <= right):
        if arr[i] <= arr[j]:
            temp[k] = arr[i]
            k += 1
            i += 1
        else:
            temp[k] = arr[j]
            k += 1
            j += 1
            inv_count += (mid - i)
    while i <= mid - 1:
        temp[k] = arr[i]
        k += 1
        i += 1
    while j <= right:
        temp[k] = arr[j]
        k += 1
        j += 1
    for idx in range(left, right + 1):
        arr[idx] = temp[idx]
    return inv_count

def _merge_sort(arr, temp, left, right):
    inv_count = 0
    if left < right:
        mid = (left + right) // 2
        inv_count += _merge_sort(arr, temp, left, mid)
        inv_count += _merge_sort(arr, temp, mid + 1, right)
        inv_count += merge(arr, temp, left, mid + 1, right)
    return inv_count

def count_inversion(arr):
    arr = list(arr)
    n = len(arr)
    temp = [0] * n
    return _merge_sort(arr, temp, 0, n - 1)

# Read input
s = input().strip()
# Handle both [ ] and ( )
if s.startswith('[') and s.endswith(']'):
    s = s[1:-1]
elif s.startswith('(') and s.endswith(')'):
    s = s[1:-1]
nums_str = [x.strip() for x in s.split(',')]
arr = [int(x) for x in nums_str if x.strip()]  # ignore empty
print(count_inversion(arr))

```python
import sys

def merge(arr, temp, left, mid, right):
    inv_count = 0
    i = left
    j = mid
    k = left
    while (i <= mid - 1) and (j <= right):
        if arr[i] <= arr[j]:
            temp[k] = arr[i]
            k += 1
            i += 1
        else:
            temp[k] = arr[j]
            k += 1
            j += 1
            inv_count += (mid - i)
    while i <= mid - 1:
        temp[k] = arr[i]
        k += 1
        i += 1
    while j <= right:
        temp[k] = arr[j]
        k += 1
        j += 1
    for idx in range(left, right + 1):
        arr[idx] = temp[idx]
    return inv_count

def _merge_sort(arr, temp, left, right):
    inv_count = 0
    if left < right:
        mid = (left + right) // 2
        inv_count += _merge_sort(arr, temp, left, mid)
        inv_count += _merge_sort(arr, temp, mid + 1, right)
        inv_count += merge(arr, temp, left, mid + 1, right)
    return inv_count

def count_inversion(arr):
    arr = list(arr)
    n = len(arr)
    temp = [0] * n
    return _merge_sort(arr, temp, 0, n - 1)

# Read input
s = input().strip()
# Handle both [ ] and ( )
if s.startswith('[') and s.endswith(']'):
    s = s[1:-1]
elif s.startswith('(') and s.endswith(')'):
    s = s[1:-1]
nums_str = [x.strip() for x in s.split(',')]
arr = [int(x) for x in nums_str if x.strip()]  # ignore empty
print(count_inversion(arr))

```python
import sys

s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
vowels = sorted(c for c in s if c in 'aeiou')
cons = sorted(c for c in s if c not in 'aeiou')
V = len(vowels)
C = len(cons)

if abs(V - C) > 1:
    print("failed")
else:
    if V == C:
        start_v = True
    elif V == C + 1:
        start_v = True
    else:
        start_v = False

    result = []
    i = j = 0
    is_v = start_v
    for _ in range(V + C):
        if is_v:
            result.append(vowels[i])
            i += 1
        else:
            result.append(cons[j])
            j += 1
        is_v = not is_v
    print(''.join(result))

vowels = sorted(c for c in s if c in 'aeiou')
cons = sorted(c for c in s if c not in 'aeiou')

C = len(cons)

if abs(V - C) > 1:
    print("failed")
else:
    if V == C:
        start_v = True
    elif V == C + 1:
        start_v = True
    else:
        start_v = False

    result = []
    i = j = 0
    is_v = start_v

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)

if n == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

prefix_pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_pipe[i + 1] = prefix_pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

left_open = [False] * n
found = False
for i in range(n):
    left_open[i] = found
    if s[i] == '[':
        found = True

right_close = [False] * n
found = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    right_close[i] = found
    if s[i] == ']':
        found = True

min_prev = n + 1
max_pipes = -1
for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == ':' and right_close[i] and min_prev <= n:
        pipes = prefix_pipe[i] - min_prev
        if pipes > max_pipes:
            max_pipes = pipes
    if s[i] == ':' and left_open[i]:
        min_prev = min(min_prev, prefix_pipe[i + 1])

if max_pipes == -1:
    print(-1)
else:
    print(4 + max_pipes)

```python
def factors(num):
    if not isinstance(num, int) or num < 1:
        return -1
    factors_list = []
    for i in range(num, 0, -1):
        if num % i == 0:
            factors_list.append(i)
    return factors_list

input_str = input().strip()
try:
    num = int(input_str)
    result = factors(num)
    print(result if result != -1 else -1)
except ValueError:
    print(-1)

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()

n = len(data)
if n == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find first '['
pos_first_open = -1
for i in range(n):
    if data[i] == '[':
        pos_first_open = i
        break

if pos_first_open == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find first ':' after pos_first_open
pos_p1 = -1
for i in range(pos_first_open + 1, n):
    if data[i] == ':':
        pos_p1 = i
        break

if pos_p1 == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find last ']'
pos_last_close = -1
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    if data[i] == ']':
        pos_last_close = i
        break

if pos_last_close == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find last ':' before pos_last_close
pos_p2 = -1
for i in range(pos_last_close - 1, -1, -1):
    if data[i] == ':':
        pos_p2 = i
        break

if pos_p2 == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

if pos_p1 >= pos_p2:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Precompute prefix for '|'
prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + (1 if data[i] == '|' else 0)

# Count '|' in [pos_p1 + 1, pos_p2 - 1]
count = prefix[pos_p2] - prefix[pos_p1 + 1]

ans = 4 + count
print(ans)

```python
import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(10**6)

def almost_everywhere_zero(n_str, k):
    s = [int(d) for d in n_str]
    L = len(s)
    memo = {}
    def dp(pos, tight, started, cnt):
        if pos == L:
            return 1 if started and cnt == k else 0
        key = (pos, tight, started, cnt)
        if key in memo:
            return memo[key]
        ans = 0
        up = s[pos] if tight else 9
        for d in range(up + 1):
            new_tight = 1 if tight and d == up else 0
            if started == 0 and d == 0:
                new_started = 0
                new_cnt = cnt
            else:
                new_started = 1
                new_cnt = cnt + (1 if d > 0 else 0)
            if new_cnt > k:
                continue
            ans += dp(pos + 1, new_tight, new_started, new_cnt)
        memo[key] = ans
        return ans
    return dp(0, 1, 0, 0)

n_str = input().strip()
k = int(input().strip())
result = almost_everywhere_zero(n_str, k)
print(result)
```

import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(10**6)

def almost_everywhere_zero(n_str, k):
    s = [int(d) for d in n_str]
    L = len(s)
    memo = {}
    def dp(pos, tight, started, cnt):
        if pos == L:
            return 1 if started and cnt == k else 0
        key = (pos, tight, started, cnt)
        if key in memo:
            return memo[key]
        ans = 0
        up = s[pos] if tight else 9
        for d in range(up + 1):
            new_tight = 1 if tight and d == up else 0
            if started == 0 and d == 0:
                new_started = 0
                new_cnt = cnt
            else:
                new_started = 1
                new_cnt = cnt + (1 if d > 0 else 0)
            if new_cnt > k:
                continue
            ans += dp(pos + 1, new_tight, new_started, new_cnt)
        memo[key] = ans
        return ans
    return dp(0, 1, 0, 0)

n_str = input().strip()
k = int(input().strip())
result = almost_everywhere_zero(n_str, k)
print(result)

import sys

s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(s)

count_bar = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    count_bar[i + 1] = count_bar[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

has_open = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    has_open[i + 1] = has_open[i] or (s[i] == '[')

has_close = [False] * (n + 1)
has_close[n] = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    has_close[i] = has_close[i + 1] or (s[i] == ']')

colons = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']
m = len(colons)

min_so_far = float('inf')
max_bars = -1

for j in range(m):
    pos = colons[j]
    if pos + 1 < n + 1 and has_close[pos + 1]:
        if min_so_far != float('inf'):
            curr = count_bar[pos] - min_so_far
            if curr > max_bars:
                max_bars = curr
    if has_open[pos]:
        this_min = count_bar[pos + 1]
        if this_min < min_so_far:
            min_so_far = this_min

if max_bars == -1:
    print(-1)
else:
    print(4 + max_bars)

def digit_value(c):
    if c.isdigit():
        return ord(c) - ord('0')
    elif 'A' <= c <= 'Z':
        return 10 + ord(c) - ord('A')

```python
import sys

def sum_of_divisor_counts(n):
    res = 0
    i = 1
    while i <= n:
        q = n // i
        r = n // q
        res += (r - i + 1) * q
        i = r + 1
    return res

input_data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = int(input_data)
print(sum_of_divisor_counts(n))

```python
s1 = input()
s2 = input()

count1 = [0] * 26
count2 = [0] * 26

for c in s1:
    if 'a' <= c <= 'z':
        count1[ord(c) - ord('a')] += 1

for c in s2:
    if 'a' <= c <= 'z':
        count2[ord(c) - ord('a')] += 1

parts = []
for i in range(26):
    c1 = count1[i]
    c2 = count2[i]
    mf = max(c1, c2)
    if mf > 1:
        letter = chr(ord('a') + i)
        if c1 > c2:
            pref = '1:'
        elif c2 > c1:
            pref = '2:'
        else:
            pref = '=:'
        part = pref + letter * mf
        parts.append(part)

parts.sort(key=lambda x: (-len(x), x))
print('/'.join(parts))

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)

if n == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

pipe_prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe_prefix[i + 1] = pipe_prefix[i] + (1 if data[i] == '|' else 0)

left_open = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    left_open[i] = left_open[i - 1] or (data[i - 1] == '[')

right_close = [False] * n
if n > 0:
    right_close[n - 1] = False
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        right_close[i] = right_close[i + 1] or (data[i + 1] == ']')

cols = [i for i in range(n) if data[i] == ':']

INF = n + 1
min_sub = INF
max_len = -1

for r in range(len(cols)):
    j = cols[r]
    if right_close[j] and min_sub < INF:
        cnt = pipe_prefix[j] - min_sub
        max_len = max(max_len, 4 + cnt)
    if left_open[j]:
        min_sub = min(min_sub, pipe_prefix[j + 1])

print(max_len if max_len != -1 else -1)

```python
import sys

def parse_num(s, d):
    s = s.replace('?', str(d))
    if not s:
        return None
    sign = 1
    orig_s = s
    if s[0] == '-':
        sign = -1
        s = s[1:]
    if not s:
        return None
    if s[0] == '0' and len(s) > 1:
        return None
    try:
        val = int(s)
        if abs(sign * val) > 1000000:
            return None
        return sign * val
    except ValueError:
        return None

def parse_expr(expr):
    i = 0
    n = len(expr)
    # Parse A
    start = 0
    if i < n and expr[i] == '-':
        i += 1
    while i < n and (expr[i].isdigit() or expr[i] == '?'):
        i += 1
    A_str = expr[start:i]
    if i == n or not A_str:
        return None
    if expr[i] not in '+-*':
        return None
    op = expr[i]
    i += 1
    # Parse B
    start = i
    if i < n and expr[i] == '-':
        i += 1
    while i < n and (expr[i].isdigit() or expr[i] == '?'):
        i += 1
    B_str = expr[start:i]
    if i == n or not B_str or i >= n or expr[i] != '=':
        return None
    i += 1  # skip =
    # Parse C
    start = i
    if i < n and expr[i] == '-':
        i += 1
    while i < n and (expr[i].isdigit() or expr[i] == '?'):
        i += 1
    C_str = expr[start:i]
    if i != n or not C_str:
        return None
    return A_str, op, B_str, C_str

expr = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if not expr:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

parts = parse_expr(expr)
if not parts:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

A_str, op, B_str, C_str = parts

known = set(c for c in expr if c.isdigit())

ans = -1
for d in range(10):
    if str(d) in known:
        continue
    a = parse_num(A_str, d)
    if a is None:
        continue
    b = parse_num(B_str, d)
    if b is None:
        continue
    c = parse_num(C_str, d)
    if c is None:
        continue
    if op == '+':
        left = a + b
    elif op == '-':
        left = a - b
    elif op == '*':
        left = a * b
    else:
        continue
    if left == c:
        ans = d
        break

print(ans)
```

import sys

if n == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

pref_pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pref_pipe[i + 1] = pref_pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

has_open = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    has_open[i] = has_open[i - 1] or (s[i - 1] == '[')

has_close_after = [False] * n
if n > 0:
    has_close_after[n - 1] = False
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        has_close_after[i] = (s[i + 1] == ']') or has_close_after[i + 1]

colons = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']

min_pref = float('inf')
max_pipes = -1

for R in colons:
    if has_close_after[R] and min_pref != float('inf'):
        pipes = pref_pipe[R] - min_pref
        if pipes > max_pipes:
            max_pipes = pipes
    if has_open[R]:
        this_pref = pref_pipe[R + 1]
        if this_pref < min_pref:
            min_pref = this_pref

if max_pipes >= 0:
    print(4 + max_pipes)
else:
    print(-1)

import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip().lower()
words = data.split()

num_dict = {
    'zero': 0, 'one': 1, 'two': 2, 'three': 3, 'four': 4,
    'five': 5, 'six': 6, 'seven': 7, 'eight': 8, 'nine': 9,
    'ten': 10,
    'eleven': 11, 'twelve': 12, 'thirteen': 13, 'fourteen': 14,
    'fifteen': 15, 'sixteen': 16, 'seventeen': 17, 'eighteen': 18, 'nineteen': 19,
    'twenty': 20, 'thirty': 30, 'forty': 40, 'fifty': 50,
    'sixty': 60, 'seventy': 70, 'eighty': 80, 'ninety': 90,
    'hundred': 100,
    'thousand': 1000,
    'million': 1000000
}

total = 0
current = 0
for word in words:
    if word == 'and':
        continue
    val = num_dict.get(word, 0)
    if val == 100:
        current *= 100
    elif val == 1000:
        total += current * 1000
        current = 0
    elif val == 1000000:
        total += current * 1000000
        current = 0
    else:
        current += val

total += current
print(total)

```python
import sys

def binom(n, k):
    if k < 0 or k > n:
        return 0
    if k == 0 or k == n:
        return 1
    k = min(k, n - k)
    res = 1
    for i in range(1, k + 1):
        res *= (n - k + i)
        res //= i
    return res

def factorize(n):
    if n == 1:
        return {}
    factors = {}
    i = 2
    while i * i <= n:
        while n % i == 0:
            factors[i] = factors.get(i, 0) + 1
            n //= i
        i += 1
    if n > 1:
        factors[n] = 1
    return factors

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()
n = int(data[0])
k = int(data[1])

factors = factorize(n)
res = 1
for e in factors.values():
    res *= binom(e + k - 1, k - 1)
print(res)

import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()

prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

min_open = n + 1
max_close = -1
for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == '[':
        min_open = min(min_open, i)
    if s[i] == ']':
        max_close = max(max_close, i)

if min_open > n or max_close < 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

m = len(colons)
if m < 2:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

while L < m and colons[L] <= min_open:
    L += 1
if L >= m:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

R = m - 1
while R >= 0 and colons[R] >= max_close:
    R -= 1
if R <= L:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

curr_min = prefix[colons[L] + 1]
for j in range(L + 1, R + 1):
    cnt = prefix[colons[j]] - curr_min
    if cnt > max_cnt:
        max_cnt = cnt
    curr_min = min(curr_min, prefix[colons[j] + 1])

import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

if n == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit()

prefix_bar = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_bar[i + 1] = prefix_bar[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

has_left = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    has_left[i] = has_left[i - 1] or (s[i - 1] == '[')

has_right = [False] * (n + 1)
has_right[n] = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    has_right[i] = (s[i] == ']') or has_right[i + 1]

colon_pos = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']
m = len(colon_pos)

min_pref = float('inf')
max_count = -1

for q in range(m):
    j = colon_pos[q]
    # Check as second colon
    if j + 1 <= n and has_right[j + 1]:
        if min_pref != float('inf'):
            count = prefix_bar[j] - min_pref
            if count > max_count:
                max_count = count
    # Update as potential first colon
    if has_left[j]:
        this_pref = prefix_bar[j + 1]
        if this_pref < min_pref:
            min_pref = this_pref

if max_count >= 0:
    print(4 + max_count)
else:
    print(-1)

import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

if n == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

prefix_has_open = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_has_open[i + 1] = prefix_has_open[i] or (s[i] == '[')

suffix_has_close = [False] * (n + 1)
suffix_has_close[n] = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    suffix_has_close[i] = suffix_has_close[i + 1] or (s[i] == ']')

prefix_pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_pipe[i + 1] = prefix_pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

min_j = -1
for j in range(n):
    if s[j] == ':' and prefix_has_open[j]:
        min_j = j
        break

if min_j == -1:
    print(-1)
else:
    max_cnt = -1
    for k in range(min_j + 1, n):
        if s[k] == ':' and (k + 1 < n + 1) and suffix_has_close[k + 1]:
            cnt = prefix_pipe[k] - prefix_pipe[min_j + 1]
            if cnt > max_cnt:
                max_cnt = cnt
    if max_cnt == -1:
        print(-1)
    else:

```python
import sys
import re
from collections import defaultdict

def parse_term(term):
    sign = 1 if term[0] == '+' else -1
    rest = term[1:]
    i = 0
    if rest and rest[0].isdigit():
        while i < len(rest) and rest[i].isdigit():
            i += 1
        coeff = int(rest[:i])
        var_str = rest[i:]
    else:
        coeff = 1
        var_str = rest
    var_list = sorted(var_str)
    key = tuple(var_list)
    return key, sign * coeff

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if data and data[0] not in '+-':
    data = '+' + data
terms = re.findall(r'([+-][^+-]+)', data)
coeff_dict = defaultdict(int)
for term in terms:
    key, tc = parse_term(term)
    coeff_dict[key] += tc
monomials = []
for key, c in coeff_dict.items():
    if c != 0:
        var_str = ''.join(key)
        deg = len(key)
        monomials.append((deg, var_str, c))
monomials.sort(key=lambda t: (t[0], t[1]))
parts = []
for i, (deg, var_str, c) in enumerate(monomials):
    abs_c = abs(c)
    if i == 0:
        sign_str = '-' if c < 0 else ''
    else:
        sign_str = '+' if c > 0 else '-'
    if deg == 0:
        coeff_part = str(abs_c)
    else:
        coeff_part = str(abs_c) if abs_c != 1 else ''
    term_str = sign_str + coeff_part + var_str
    parts.append(term_str)
output = ''.join(parts)
print(output)
```

```python
import sys
import ast

def solution(text, markers):
    lines = text.splitlines()
    result_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        min_pos = len(line)
        for m in markers:
            pos = line.find(m)
            if pos != -1:
                min_pos = min(min_pos, pos)
        if min_pos == len(line):
            stripped = line.rstrip()
        else:
            stripped = line[:min_pos].rstrip()
        result_lines.append(stripped)
    return '\n'.join(result_lines)

data = sys.stdin.read().splitlines()
markers_str = data[-1]
text = '\n'.join(data[:-1])
markers = ast.literal_eval(markers_str)
result = solution(text, markers)
print(result)

    a = [int(x) for x in nums_str if x.strip()]
else:
    a = []

if not a:
    print(0)
    sys.exit(0)

g = reduce(gcd, a)
if g != 1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

if min(a) == 1:
    print(0)
    sys.exit(0)

dp = [False] * SIZE
dp[0] = True

for coin in a:
    for j in range(coin, SIZE):
        dp[j] = dp[j] or dp[j - coin]

ans = 0
for i in range(1, SIZE):
    if not dp[i]:
        ans = i

print(ans)

```python
import sys

def next_smaller(s):
    if len(s) < 2:
        return -1
    digits = list(s)
    n = len(digits)
    # Find rightmost k where digits[k] > digits[k+1]
    k = -1
    for i in range(n-2, -1, -1):
        if digits[i] > digits[i+1]:
            k = i
            break
    if k == -1:
        return -1
    # Find rightmost l > k where digits[l] < digits[k]
    l = -1
    for i in range(n-1, k, -1):
        if digits[i] < digits[k]:
            l = i
            break
    # Swap
    digits[k], digits[l] = digits[l], digits[k]
    # Reverse k+1 to end
    left, right = k + 1, n - 1
    while left < right:
        digits[left], digits[right] = digits[right], digits[left]
        left += 1
        right -= 1
    # Check leading zero
    if digits[0] == '0':
        return -1
    return ''.join(digits)

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if not data or not data.isdigit():
    print(-1)
else:
    result = next_smaller(data)
    print(result)

import sys

def binom(n, k):
    if k > n or k < 0:
        return 0
    res = 1
    for i in range(k):
        res *= (n - i)
        res //= (i + 1)
    return res

input = sys.stdin.read

x = int(data)

a = binom(x + 9, 9)
b = binom(x + 10, 10)
result = a + b - 10 * x - 1
print(result)

```python
import sys
import math

def is_perfect_square(x):
    if x < 0:
        return False
    s = int(math.sqrt(x))
    return s * s == x

def min_squares(n):
    # Check for 1 square
    if is_perfect_square(n):
        return 1
    
    # Check for 2 squares
    sq = int(math.sqrt(n)) + 1
    for i in range(1, sq):
        if is_perfect_square(n - i * i):
            return 2
    
    # Check for 3 squares using Legendre's three-square theorem
    m = n
    while m % 4 == 0:
        m //= 4
    if m % 8 != 7:
        return 3
    
    # Must be 4
    return 4

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()
n = int(data)
print(min_squares(n))
```

```python
def exp_sum(n):
    if n == 0:
        return 1
    p = [0] * (n + 1)
    p[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        for j in range(i, n + 1):
            p[j] += p[j - i]
    return p[n]

n = int(input())
print(exp_sum(n))

completed 70/150, Solved: False, number of success = 11/70, acc = 15.71
```python
def next_bigger(num: str) -> str:
    digits = list(num)
    n = len(digits)
    
    # Step 1: Find the pivot point (rightmost i where digits[i] < digits[i+1])
    i = n - 2
    while i >= 0 and digits[i] >= digits[i + 1]:
        i -= 1
    
    # If no such i, it's the last permutation
    if i < 0:
        return "-1"
    
    # Step 2: Find the smallest digit to the right of i that is greater than digits[i]
    j = n - 1
    while digits[j] <= digits[i]:
        j -= 1
    
    # Step 3: Swap digits[i] and digits[j]
    digits[i], digits[j] = digits[j], digits[i]
    
    # Step 4: Reverse the suffix from i+1 to the end
    digits[i + 1:] = reversed(digits[i + 1:])
    
    # Join and return (no leading zeros possible for next larger permutation)
    return "".join(digits)

# Read input
s = input().strip()

# Call function and print result
result = next_bigger(s)
print(result)
```

## Explanation

1. **Input Handling**: Read the input string `s` representing the number.
2. **Convert to List**: Treat the string as a list of digits for easy manipulation.
3. **Find Pivot (`i`)**: Traverse from the second-to-last digit leftward to find the first position where the digit is smaller than the next one. This is the "pivot" for the next permutation.
4. **Check Feasibility**: If no such pivot exists (sequence is non-increasing), no larger permutation exists; return `"-1"`.
5. **Find Successor (`j`)**: From the end, find the smallest digit larger than the pivot digit.
6. **Swap**: Exchange the pivot and successor digits.
7. **Reverse Suffix**: Reverse all digits after the pivot to get the smallest possible next permutation.
8. **Output**: Join the digits into a string and print. The result is guaranteed larger than the input and without leading zeros (since input has none and it's the next larger arrangement). 

This algorithm runs in O(n) time, efficient for numbers up to 18 digits (10^18). 

**Verification with Examples**:
- `12` → `21` (pivot at 1<'2', swap → `21`)
- `513` → `531` (pivot at 1<'3', successor 3, swap & reverse → `531`)
- `2017` → `2071` (pivot at 0<'1', successor 1, swap & reverse → `2071`)
- `9` → `"-1"` (no pivot)
- `111` → `"-1"` (no pivot)
- `531` → `"-1"` (no pivot)
```python
def next_bigger(num: str) -> str:
    digits = list(num)
    n = len(digits)
    
    # Step 1: Find the pivot point (rightmost i where digits[i] < digits[i+1])
    i = n - 2
    while i >= 0 and digits[i] >= digits[i + 1]:
        i -= 1
    
    # If no such i, it's the last permutation
    if i < 0:
        return "-1"
    
    # Step 2: Find the smallest digit to the right of i that is greater than digits[i]
    j = n - 1
    while digits[j] <= digits[i]:
        j -= 1
    
    # Step 3: Swap digits[i] and digits[j]
    digits[i], digits[j] = digits[j], digits[i]
    
    # Step 4: Reverse the suffix from i+1 to the end
    digits[i + 1:] = reversed(digits[i + 1:])
    
    # Join and return (no leading zeros possible for next larger permutation)
    return "".join(digits)

# Read input
s = input().strip()

# Call function and print result
result = next_bigger(s)
print(result)
```

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = int(data)

greens = []
a5 = 5
a6 = 6
current_mod = 10
a1 = 1
max_needed = n + 10
d = 1

while len(greens) < max_needed:
    powdm1 = 1 if d == 1 else 10 ** (d - 1)
    candidates = []
    if a1 >= powdm1 and a1 > 0:
        candidates.append(str(a1))
    if a5 >= powdm1 and a5 > 0:
        candidates.append(str(a5))
    if a6 >= powdm1 and a6 > 0:
        candidates.append(str(a6))
    greens.extend(candidates)

    next_mod = current_mod * 10

    # lift a5
    sq = pow(a5, 2, next_mod)
    r = (sq - a5) // current_mod
    c = (2 * a5 - 1) % 10
    target = (-r) % 10
    t_found = None
    for t in range(10):
        if (t * c) % 10 == target:
            t_found = t
            break
    a5 = a5 + t_found * current_mod

    # lift a6
    sq = pow(a6, 2, next_mod)
    r = (sq - a6) // current_mod
    c = (2 * a6 - 1) % 10
    target = (-r) % 10
    t_found = None
    for t in range(10):
        if (t * c) % 10 == target:
            t_found = t
            break
    a6 = a6 + t_found * current_mod

    current_mod = next_mod
    d += 1
    if d > 10000:
        break

greens.sort(key=lambda s: (len(s), s))
print(greens[n - 1])

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

# cnt_pipe[i] = number of '|' in positions 0 to i-1
cnt_pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    cnt_pipe[i + 1] = cnt_pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

# has_open[i] = True if there is '[' in 0..i-1
has_open = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    has_open[i] = has_open[i - 1] or (s[i - 1] == '[')

# has_close[i] = True if there is ']' in i..n-1
has_close = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    has_close[i] = has_close[i + 1] or (s[i] == ']')

# collect colon positions
cols = [i for i in range(n) if s[i] == ':']

min_prev = float('inf')
max_len = -1

for q in cols:
    # check as second colon
    if q + 1 <= n and has_close[q + 1]:
        if min_prev != float('inf'):
            count = cnt_pipe[q] - min_prev
            max_len = max(max_len, 4 + count)
    # check as first colon
    if has_open[q]:
        p1 = q + 1
        min_prev = min(min_prev, cnt_pipe[p1])

print(max_len)

import sys
import ast

transitions = {
    "CLOSED": {
        "APP_PASSIVE_OPEN": "LISTEN",
        "APP_ACTIVE_OPEN": "SYN_SENT"
    },
    "LISTEN": {
        "RCV_SYN": "SYN_RCVD",
        "APP_SEND": "SYN_SENT",
        "APP_CLOSE": "CLOSED"
    },
    "SYN_RCVD": {
        "APP_CLOSE": "FIN_WAIT_1",
        "RCV_ACK": "ESTABLISHED"
    },
    "SYN_SENT": {
        "RCV_SYN": "SYN_RCVD",
        "RCV_SYN_ACK": "ESTABLISHED",
        "APP_CLOSE": "CLOSED"
    },
    "ESTABLISHED": {
        "APP_CLOSE": "FIN_WAIT_1",
        "RCV_FIN": "CLOSE_WAIT"
    },
    "FIN_WAIT_1": {
        "RCV_FIN": "CLOSING",
        "RCV_FIN_ACK": "TIME_WAIT",
        "RCV_ACK": "FIN_WAIT_2"
    },
    "CLOSING": {
        "RCV_ACK": "TIME_WAIT"
    },
    "FIN_WAIT_2": {
        "RCV_FIN": "TIME_WAIT"
    },
    "TIME_WAIT": {
        "APP_TIMEOUT": "CLOSED"
    },
    "CLOSE_WAIT": {
        "APP_CLOSE": "LAST_ACK"
    },
    "LAST_ACK": {
        "RCV_ACK": "CLOSED"
    }
}

events_str = sys.stdin.read().strip()
events = ast.literal_eval(events_str)

current = "CLOSED"
for event in events:
    if current in transitions and event in transitions[current]:
        current = transitions[current][event]
    else:
        print("ERROR")
        sys.exit(0)

print(current)

```python
def count_change(amount, coins):
    dp = [0] * (amount + 1)
    dp[0] = 1
    for coin in coins:
        for i in range(coin, amount + 1):
            dp[i] += dp[i - coin]
    return dp[amount]

amount = int(input())
coins_str = input().strip()
coins = [int(x) for x in coins_str[1:-1].split(',')]
print(count_change(amount, coins))

def proper_fractions(n):
    if n < 2:
        return 0

```python
def proper_fractions(n):
    if n < 2:
        return 0
    phi = n
    if n % 2 == 0:
        phi -= phi // 2
        while n % 2 == 0:
            n //= 2
    i = 3
    while i * i <= n:
        if n % i == 0:
            phi -= phi // i
            while n % i == 0:
                n //= i
        i += 2
    if n > 1:
        phi -= phi // n
    return phi

n = int(input().strip())
print(proper_fractions(n))

```python
import sys

MOD = 1000000007

class Fenwick:
    def __init__(self, size):
        self.size = size
        self.tree = [0] * (size + 2)

    def update(self, idx, val):
        val %= MOD
        while idx <= self.size:
            self.tree[idx] = (self.tree[idx] + val) % MOD
            idx += idx & -idx

    def prefix(self, idx):
        res = 0
        while idx > 0:
            res = (res + self.tree[idx]) % MOD
            idx -= idx & -idx
        return res

lines = sys.stdin.readlines()
line_idx = 0
n, m = map(int, lines[line_idx].strip().split())
line_idx += 1

grid = [[0 for _ in range(m + 2)] for _ in range(n + 2)]
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    s = lines[line_idx].strip()
    line_idx += 1
    for j in range(1, m + 1):
        grid[i][j] = 1 if s[j - 1] == 'R' else 0

suffix_row = [[0 for _ in range(m + 2)] for _ in range(n + 2)]
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    suffix_row[i][m + 1] = 0
    for j in range(m, 0, -1):
        suffix_row[i][j] = suffix_row[i][j + 1] + grid[i][j]

suffix_col = [[0 for _ in range(n + 2)] for _ in range(m + 2)]
for j in range(1, m + 1):
    suffix_col[j][n + 1] = 0
    for i in range(n, 0, -1):
        suffix_col[j][i] = suffix_col[j][i + 1] + grid[i][j]

dp = [[0 for _ in range(m + 2)] for _ in range(n + 2)]

fen_col = [Fenwick(n + 2) for _ in range(m + 2)]

for i in range(1, n + 1):
    fen_row = Fenwick(m + 2)
    for j in range(1, m + 1):
        from_left = fen_row.prefix(j)
        from_up = fen_col[j].prefix(i)
        extra = 1 if i == 1 and j == 1 else 0
        dp[i][j] = (from_left + from_up + extra) % MOD

        # propagate row
        s_row = suffix_row[i][j + 1]
        maxr_row = m - s_row
        fen_row.update(j, dp[i][j])
        if maxr_row + 1 <= m + 1:
            fen_row.update(maxr_row + 1, (MOD - dp[i][j]) % MOD)

        # propagate col
        s_col = suffix_col[j][i + 1]
        maxr_col = n - s_col
        fen_col[j].update(i, dp[i][j])
        if maxr_col + 1 <= n + 1:
            fen_col[j].update(maxr_col + 1, (MOD - dp[i][j]) % MOD)

print(dp[n][m])

            i += 1
            continue
        if s[i] == '-':

```python
def bowlingScore(frames_str):
    def parse_frame(s):
        fr = []
        for c in s:
            if c == 'X':
                fr.append(10)
            elif c == '-':
                fr.append(0)
            elif c.isdigit():
                fr.append(int(c))
            elif c == '/':
                prev = fr[-1]
                fr.append(10 - prev)
        return fr
    
    frames = frames_str.split()
    rolls = []
    for frame_str in frames:
        rolls.extend(parse_frame(frame_str))
    
    score = 0
    roll_index = 0
    for frame in range(1, 11):
        if frame < 10:
            first = rolls[roll_index]
            if first == 10:
                score += 10 + rolls[roll_index + 1] + rolls[roll_index + 2]
                roll_index += 1
            else:
                second = rolls[roll_index + 1]
                if first + second == 10:
                    score += 10 + rolls[roll_index + 2]
                else:
                    score += first + second
                roll_index += 2
        else:
            score += sum(rolls[roll_index:])
    return score

s = input().strip()
print(bowlingScore(s))

```python
import sys

s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(s)

# Find first '['
first_open = -1
for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == '[':
        first_open = i
        break

if first_open == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find last ']'
last_close = -1
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    if s[i] == ']':
        last_close = i
        break

if last_close == -1:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Prefix sum for '|'
pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe[i + 1] = pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

# Collect colon positions
cols = []
for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == ':':
        cols.append(i)

m = len(cols)
if m < 2:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find start: first colon after first_open
start = 0
while start < m and cols[start] <= first_open:
    start += 1

if start == m:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find end: last colon before last_close
end = m - 1
while end >= 0 and cols[end] >= last_close:
    end -= 1

if end < start:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# If same colon
if start == end:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Now compute pipes between cols[start] and cols[end]
first_c = cols[start]
sec_c = cols[end]
pipes = pipe[sec_c] - pipe[first_c + 1]

ans = 4 + pipes
print(ans)

import sys

digits_str = sys.stdin.readline().strip()
digits = int(digits_str)

# Parse x_str to Fraction
if '.' in x_str:
    dot_pos = x_str.index('.')
    num_str = x_str.replace('.', '')
    dec_places = len(x_str) - dot_pos - 1
    x = Fraction(int(num_str), 10 ** dec_places)
else:
    x = Fraction(int(x_str), 1)

current = Fraction(1)
term = Fraction(1)
n = 1
num_digits = 1

while num_digits < digits:
    term = term * x / n
    if term == 0:
        break
    current += term
    num_digits = len(str(abs(current.numerator)))
    n += 1

print(f'[{current.numerator},{current.denominator}]')
