```python
def total_digits(n):
    if n < 1:
        return 0
    res = 0
    d = 1
    power = 1
    while power <= n:
        low = power
        high = min(n, power * 10 - 1)
        count = high - low + 1
        res += count * d
        d += 1
        power *= 10
    return res

def sum_j_digits(n):
    if n < 1:
        return 0
    res = 0
    d = 1
    power = 1
    while power <= n:
        low = power
        high = min(n, power * 10 - 1)
        count = high - low + 1
        sumj = (low + high) * count // 2
        res += sumj * d
        d += 1
        power *= 10
    return res

def cum_length(b):
    if b < 1:
        return 0
    D = total_digits(b)
    T = sum_j_digits(b)
    return (b + 1) * D - T

def find_block(n):
    low = 1
    high = 2 * 10**9
    while low < high:
        mid = (low + high) // 2
        if cum_length(mid) >= n:
            high = mid
        else:
            low = mid + 1
    return low

def find_number(pos, maxj):
    low = 1
    high = maxj
    while low < high:
        mid = (low + high) // 2
        if total_digits(mid) >= pos:
            high = mid
        else:
            low = mid + 1
    return low

n = int(input())
b = find_block(n)
prev_cum = cum_length(b - 1)
pos = n - prev_cum
j = find_number(pos, b)
prev_d = total_digits(j - 1)
offset = pos - prev_d
strj = str(j)
char = strj[offset - 1]
print(char)
```

        count = high - low + 1
        sumj = (low + high) * count // 2
        res += sumj * d
        d += 1
        power *= 10
    return res

    if b < 1:
        return 0
    D = total_digits(b)
    T = sum_j_digits(b)
    return (b + 1) * D - T

    while low < high:
        mid = (low + high) // 2
        if cum_length(mid) >= n:
            high = mid

            low = mid + 1
    return low

    high = maxj
    while low < high:
        mid = (low + high) // 2
        if total_digits(mid) >= pos:
            high = mid
        else:
            low = mid + 1
    return low

```python
import sys

def min_swaps_to_sort(sequence):
    n = len(sequence)
    count7 = 0
    count8 = 0
    count9 = 0
    for val in sequence:
        if val == 7:
            count7 += 1
        elif val == 8:
            count8 += 1
        elif val == 9:
            count9 += 1
    p = count7
    q = count8
    r = count9

    l7 = l8 = l9 = 0
    m7 = m8 = m9 = 0
    r7 = r8 = r9 = 0

    for i in range(n):
        val = sequence[i]
        if i < p:
            if val == 7:
                l7 += 1
            elif val == 8:
                l8 += 1
            else:
                l9 += 1
        elif i < p + q:
            if val == 7:
                m7 += 1
            elif val == 8:
                m8 += 1
            else:
                m9 += 1
        else:
            if val == 7:
                r7 += 1
            elif val == 8:
                r8 += 1
            else:
                r9 += 1

    u = m7
    w = r7
    x = l8
    y = l9
    v = m9
    z = r8

    p1 = min(u, x)
    p2 = min(w, y)
    p3 = min(z, v)

    q1 = min(max(u - x, 0), max(z - v, 0), max(y - w, 0))
    q2 = min(max(w - y, 0), max(v - z, 0), max(x - u, 0))

    c_sub = p1 + p2 + p3 + q1 + q2

    k = x + y + u + v + w + z

    return k - c_sub

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if data.startswith('[') and data.endswith(']'):
    data = data[1:-1]
seq_str = data.split(',')
sequence = []
for ss in seq_str:
    sequence.append(int(ss.strip()))

print(min_swaps_to_sort(sequence))
```

import sys

def min_swaps_to_sort(sequence):
    n = len(sequence)
    count7 = 0
    count8 = 0
    count9 = 0
    for val in sequence:
        if val == 7:
            count7 += 1
        elif val == 8:
            count8 += 1
        elif val == 9:
            count9 += 1
    p = count7
    q = count8
    r = count9

    l7 = l8 = l9 = 0
    m7 = m8 = m9 = 0
    r7 = r8 = r9 = 0

    for i in range(n):
        val = sequence[i]
        if i < p:
            if val == 7:
                l7 += 1
            elif val == 8:
                l8 += 1
            else:
                l9 += 1
        elif i < p + q:
            if val == 7:
                m7 += 1
            elif val == 8:
                m8 += 1
            else:
                m9 += 1
        else:
            if val == 7:
                r7 += 1
            elif val == 8:
                r8 += 1
            else:
                r9 += 1

    u = m7
    w = r7
    x = l8
    y = l9
    v = m9
    z = r8

    p1 = min(u, x)
    p2 = min(w, y)
    p3 = min(z, v)

    q1 = min(max(u - x, 0), max(z - v, 0), max(y - w, 0))
    q2 = min(max(w - y, 0), max(v - z, 0), max(x - u, 0))

    c_sub = p1 + p2 + p3 + q1 + q2

    k = x + y + u + v + w + z

    return k - c_sub

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
if data.startswith('[') and data.endswith(']'):
    data = data[1:-1]
seq_str = data.split(',')
sequence = []
for ss in seq_str:
    sequence.append(int(ss.strip()))

print(min_swaps_to_sort(sequence))
```

```python
import re
import sys

def parse_term(term_str):
    term_str = term_str.strip()
    sign = 1
    if term_str.startswith('+'):
        term_str = term_str[1:].strip()
    elif term_str.startswith('-'):
        sign = -1
        term_str = term_str[1:].strip()
    
    if not term_str:
        return 0, 0
    
    if 'x' not in term_str:
        coeff = int(term_str)
        power = 0
    else:
        parts = term_str.split('x')
        if len(parts) != 2:
            return 0, 0  # invalid, treat as 0
        before = parts[0].strip()
        after = parts[1].strip()
        if before == '':
            coeff = 1
        else:
            coeff = int(before)
        if after == '':
            power = 1
        elif after.startswith('^'):
            power_str = after[1:]
            power = int(power_str) if power_str else 0
        else:
            power = 0  # invalid
        coeff *= sign
        power = int(power)
    return coeff, power

def differentiate(poly, x_val):
    terms_str = re.findall(r'[+-]?[^+-]+', poly)
    deriv = 0
    for t in terms_str:
        coeff, power = parse_term(t)
        if power > 0:
            deriv += coeff * power * (x_val ** (power - 1))
    return deriv

# Read input
poly = input().strip()
x_val = int(input().strip())
print(differentiate(poly, x_val))
```
```python
import re

def parse_term(term_str):
    term_str = term_str.strip()
    sign = 1
    if term_str.startswith('+'):
        term_str = term_str[1:].strip()
    elif term_str.startswith('-'):
        sign = -1
        term_str = term_str[1:].strip()
    
    if not term_str:
        return 0, 0
    
    if 'x' not in term_str:
        coeff = sign * int(term_str)
        power = 0
    else:
        parts = term_str.split('x')
        if len(parts) != 2:
            return 0, 0  # invalid, treat as 0
        before = parts[0].strip()
        after = parts[1].strip()
        if before == '':
            coeff = 1
        else:
            coeff = int(before)
        if after == '':
            power = 1
        elif after.startswith('^'):
            power_str = after[1:]
            power = int(power_str) if power_str else 0
        else:
            power = 0  # invalid
        coeff *= sign
        power = int(power)
    return coeff, power

def differentiate(poly, x_val):
    terms_str = re.findall(r'[+-]?[^+-]+', poly)
    deriv = 0
    for t in terms_str:
        coeff, power = parse_term(t)
        if power > 0:
            deriv += coeff * power * (x_val ** (power - 1))
    return deriv

# Read input
poly = input().strip()
x_val = int(input().strip())
print(differentiate(poly, x_val))

```python
import sys

def longest_palindrome(s):
    if not s:
        return ""
    t = '^#' + '#'.join(s) + '#$'
    n = len(t)
    P = [0] * n
    C = 0
    R = 0
    best_length = 0
    best_start = 0
    for i in range(1, n - 1):
        if i < R:
            mirr = 2 * C - i
            P[i] = min(R - i, P[mirr])
        # Expand
        while (i - P[i] - 1 >= 0 and
               i + P[i] + 1 < n and
               t[i + P[i] + 1] == t[i - P[i] - 1]):
            P[i] += 1
        if i + P[i] > R:
            C = i
            R = i + P[i]
        # Check for best
        orig_len = P[i]
        orig_start = (i - P[i]) // 2
        if (orig_len > best_length or
            (orig_len == best_length and orig_start < best_start)):
            best_length = orig_len
            best_start = orig_start
    return s[best_start:best_start + best_length]

s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
print(longest_palindrome(s))
```

## Explanation

Manacher's algorithm finds the longest palindromic substring in linear time by transforming the string and using dynamic programming with mirroring.

1. **String Transformation**: Insert '#' between characters of `s` and add sentinels '^' at the start and '$' at the end. This handles even/odd-length palindromes uniformly and prevents boundary issues. For `s = "babad"`, `t = "^#b#a#b#a#d#$"`.

2. **P Array Initialization**: `P[i]` stores the radius of the longest palindrome centered at `t[i]`. The original palindrome length equals `P[i]`.

3. **Mirroring and Expansion**:
   - Maintain center `C` and right boundary `R` of the current palindrome region.
   - For each position `i`, if `i < R`, initialize `P[i]` using the mirror position across `C` to avoid recomputation.
   - Expand around `i` by comparing characters `t[i + P[i] + 1]` and `t[i - P[i] - 1]` while within bounds.

4. **Tracking the Best Palindrome**:
   - For each `i`, compute original start index `(i - P[i]) // 2` and length `P[i]`.
   - Update the best if this length is greater, or equal but starts earlier (ensures leftmost).

5. **Extraction**: Slice `s` using the best start and length.

This achieves O(N) time as each expansion across all centers covers the string at most twice due to mirroring.
```python
import sys

def longest_palindrome(s):
    if not s:
        return ""
    t = '^#' + '#'.join(s) + '#$'
    n = len(t)
    P = [0] * n
    C = 0
    R = 0
    best_length = 0
    best_start = 0
    for i in range(1, n - 1):
        if i < R:
            mirr = 2 * C - i
            P[i] = min(R - i, P[mirr])
        # Expand
        while (i - P[i] - 1 >= 0 and
               i + P[i] + 1 < n and
               t[i + P[i] + 1] == t[i - P[i] - 1]):
            P[i] += 1
        if i + P[i] > R:
            C = i
            R = i + P[i]
        # Check for best
        orig_len = P[i]
        orig_start = (i - P[i]) // 2
        if (orig_len > best_length or
            (orig_len == best_length and orig_start < best_start)):
            best_length = orig_len
            best_start = orig_start
    return s[best_start:best_start + best_length]

s = sys.stdin.read().strip()
print(longest_palindrome(s))

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
n = int(data[0])
a = list(map(int, data[1:1 + n]))

pairs = [(a[i], i) for i in range(n)]
pairs.sort()

dest = [0] * n
for rank in range(n):
    orig_i = pairs[rank][1]
    dest[orig_i] = rank

visited = [False] * n
cycles = []
for start in range(n):
    if not visited[start]:
        cycle = []
        x = start
        while not visited[x]:
            visited[x] = True
            cycle.append(x)
            x = dest[x]
        cycles.append(cycle)

print(len(cycles))
for cycle in cycles:
    print(len(cycle), *(i + 1 for i in cycle))

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
m = int(data[index])
index += 1

parties = [[] for _ in range(m + 1)]
for i in range(n):
    p = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    c = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    parties[p].append(c)

init1 = len(parties[1])

for j in range(1, m + 1):
    parties[j].sort()

ans = float('inf')
N = n + 5  # safe upper bound

for t in range(N):
    mand_k = 0
    mand_cost = 0
    extras = []
    for j in range(2, m + 1):
        sj = len(parties[j])
        excess = max(0, sj - t)
        mand_k += excess
        for ii in range(excess):
            mand_cost += parties[j][ii]
        for ii in range(excess, sj):
            extras.append(parties[j][ii])
    k = t + 1 - init1
    if k < 0:
        continue
    if mand_k > k:
        continue
    add_k = k - mand_k
    if add_k > len(extras):
        continue
    extras.sort()
    add_cost = 0
    for i in range(add_k):
        add_cost += extras[i]
    total_cost = mand_cost + add_cost
    if total_cost < ans:
        ans = total_cost

print(int(ans))

```python
import sys

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
m = int(data[index])
index += 1

parties = [[] for _ in range(m + 1)]
for i in range(n):
    p = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    c = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    parties[p].append(c)

init1 = len(parties[1])

for j in range(1, m + 1):
    parties[j].sort()

ans = float('inf')

for t in range(n + 1):
    mand_k = 0
    mand_cost = 0
    extras = []
    for j in range(2, m + 1):
        sj = len(parties[j])
        excess = max(0, sj - t)
        mand_k += excess
        for ii in range(excess):
            mand_cost += parties[j][ii]
        for ii in range(excess, sj):
            extras.append(parties[j][ii])
    needed = max(0, t + 1 - init1 - mand_k)
    if needed > len(extras):
        continue
    extras.sort()
    add_cost = 0
    for i in range(needed):
        add_cost += extras[i]
    total_cost = mand_cost + add_cost
    if total_cost < ans:
        ans = total_cost

print(int(ans))

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
t = int(data[index])
index += 1

for _ in range(t):
    n = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    a = []
    for j in range(n):
        a.append(int(data[index]))
        index += 1
    
    p = sum(1 for x in a if x == 1)
    q = n - p
    
    if q == 0:
        if p % 2 == 0:
            print("HL")
        else:
            print("T")
    elif q == 1:
        b = next(x for x in a if x >= 2)
        if b == p:
            print("HL")
        else:
            print("T")
    else:
        bigs = [x for x in a if x >= 2]
        m = max(bigs)
        r = sum(1 for x in bigs if x == m)
        if r == q and p == 0:
            print("HL")
        else:
            print("T")
```

## Explanation

The provided code determines the winner of each game based on the following analysis of optimal play:

1. **Count piles of size 1 (p) and piles ≥2 (q = n - p)**:
   - `p`: Number of piles with exactly 1 stone.
   - `q`: Number of piles with ≥2 stones.

2. **Case q == 0 (all piles size 1)**:
   - The game reduces to emptying piles one by one with no restrictions after the first move.
   - First player wins if p is odd (takes the last pile); second wins if even.

3. **Case q == 1 (exactly one pile ≥2 with size b, p piles of 1)**:
   - First player can force second to empty 1-piles by repeatedly playing in the large pile.
   - This mirrors a game where first effectively plays second in the subgame of p 1-piles, adjusted by b moves.
   - Second wins exactly when b == p (symmetric loss for first).

4. **Case q ≥ 2 (multiple piles ≥2)**:
   - First player wins unless all q piles have identical size m and p == 0.
   - In this symmetric case (all equal size ≥2, no 1-piles), second player uses a mirroring strategy across piles to force first into a loss.
   - Otherwise (different sizes among big piles, or p > 0), first can disrupt symmetry (e.g., empty a 1-pile or reduce a unique largest pile) to reach a losing position for second.

This classification covers all cases, matching simulations and samples:
- n=1, [2]: q=1, p=0, b=2 ≠0 → T
- n=2, [1,1]: q=0, p=2 even → HL

    if q == 0:
        if p % 2 == 0:
            print("HL")

            print("T")
    elif q == 1:

            print("HL")
        else:
            print("T")

        bigs = [x for x in a if x >= 2]
        m = max(bigs)
        r = sum(1 for x in bigs if x == m)

            print("HL")
        else:
            print("T")

```python
import sys

class UF:
    def __init__(self, n):
        self.p = list(range(n))
        self.rank = [0] * n

    def union(self, x, y):
        px = self.find(x)
        py = self.find(y)
        if px == py:
            return
        if self.rank[px] < self.rank[py]:
            self.p[px] = py
        elif self.rank[px] > self.rank[py]:
            self.p[py] = px
        else:
            self.p[py] = px
            self.rank[px] += 1

    def find(self, x):
        if self.p[x] != x:
            self.p[x] = self.find(self.p[x])
        return self.p[x]

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
m = int(data[index])
index += 1

lang_users = [[] for _ in range(m + 1)]
has_any = False

for i in range(n):
    k = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    for _ in range(k):
        a = int(data[index])
        index += 1
        lang_users[a].append(i)
    if k > 0:
        has_any = True

uf = UF(n)

for l in range(1, m + 1):
    users = lang_users[l]
    if len(users) >= 2:
        first = users[0]
        for j in range(1, len(users)):
            uf.union(first, users[j])

comps = set()
for i in range(n):
    comps.add(uf.find(i))

c = len(comps)

if c == 1:
    print(0)
elif has_any:
    print(c - 1)
else:
    print(c)
```

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
a = [int(data[index + i]) for i in range(n)]
index += n
q = int(data[index])
index += 1

events = []
for _ in range(q):
    typ = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    if typ == 1:
        p = int(data[index])
        index += 1
        x = int(data[index])
        index += 1
        events.append((1, p, x))
    else:
        x = int(data[index])
        index += 1
        events.append((2, x))

last_time = [0] * (n + 1)
last_val = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    last_val[i] = a[i - 1]

for t in range(1, q + 1):
    ev = events[t - 1]
    if ev[0] == 1:
        p = ev[1]
        x = ev[2]
        last_time[p] = t
        last_val[p] = x

max_after = [0] * (q + 1)
cur_max = 0
for t in range(q, -1, -1):
    max_after[t] = cur_max
    if t >= 1:
        ev = events[t - 1]
        if ev[0] == 2:
            cur_max = max(cur_max, ev[1])

final = []
for p in range(1, n + 1):
    t = last_time[p]
    mx = max_after[t]
    val = max(last_val[p], mx)
    final.append(str(val))

print(' '.join(final))

completed 106/150, Solved: True, number of success = 20/106, acc = 18.87
```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)

left_open = n + 1
right_close = -1
colon_pos = []

for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == '[':
        left_open = min(left_open, i)
    elif s[i] == ']':
        right_close = max(right_close, i)
    elif s[i] == ':':
        colon_pos.append(i)

if left_open > n or right_close < 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

m = len(colon_pos)
if m == 0:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find L: first colon after left_open
L = 0
while L < m and colon_pos[L] <= left_open:
    L += 1
if L == m:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Find R_max: last colon before right_close
R_max = m - 1
while R_max >= L and colon_pos[R_max] >= right_close:
    R_max -= 1
if R_max < L:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

first_pos = colon_pos[L]
second_pos = colon_pos[R_max]

if first_pos >= second_pos:
    print(-1)
    sys.exit(0)

# Compute prefix for |
pipe_prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe_prefix[i + 1] = pipe_prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

pipes = pipe_prefix[second_pos] - pipe_prefix[first_pos + 1]
print(4 + pipes)

import sys

data = input().split()

n = int(data[0])

z00 = z01 = z10 = z11 = 0
for i in range(n):
    if a[i] == '0':
        if b[i] == '0':
            z00 += 1
        else:
            z01 += 1
    else:
        if b[i] == '0':
            z10 += 1
        else:
            z11 += 1

a0 = z00 + z01
a1 = z10 + z11
total_mixed = a0 * a1
bad = z01 * z11
ans = total_mixed - bad

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

n = int(data[0])
h = [0] * (n + 2)
index = 1
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    h[i] = int(data[index])
    index += 1
# h[0] = 0, h[n+1] = 0 already set

lm = [0] * (n + 2)
lm[0] = h[0] - 0
for i in range(1, n + 2):
    lm[i] = min(lm[i - 1], h[i] - i)

rm = [0] * (n + 2)
rm[n + 1] = h[n + 1] + (n + 1)
for i in range(n, -1, -1):
    rm[i] = min(rm[i + 1], h[i] + i)

ans = 0
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    leftv = i + lm[i]
    rightv = rm[i] - i
    fi = min(leftv, rightv)
    if fi > ans:
        ans = fi

print(ans)

completed 108/150, Solved: True, number of success = 22/108, acc = 20.37
```python
import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(400000)

def get_transfer(om):
    f = [0] * 4
    for ins in range(4):
        inc = 0
        if (ins & 1) and (om & 1):
            inc |= 1
        if (ins & 2) and (om & 2):
            inc |= 2
        out = inc
        if om == 3 and inc != 0:
            out = 3
        f[ins] = out
    return tuple(f)

def compose(g, f):
    return tuple(g[f[i]] for i in range(4))

def build(node, start, end, is_open, tree):
    if start == end:
        col = start + 1
        om = (1 if is_open[0][col] else 0) | (2 if is_open[1][col] else 0)
        tree[node] = get_transfer(om)
        return
    mid = (start + end) // 2
    build(2 * node, start, mid, is_open, tree)
    build(2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end, is_open, tree)
    tree[node] = compose(tree[2 * node + 1], tree[2 * node])

def update(node, start, end, idx, newf, tree):
    if start == end:
        tree[node] = newf
        return
    mid = (start + end) // 2
    if idx <= mid:
        update(2 * node, start, mid, idx, newf, tree)
    else:
        update(2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end, idx, newf, tree)
    tree[node] = compose(tree[2 * node + 1], tree[2 * node])

def main():
    input = sys.stdin.read
    data = input().split()
    index = 0
    n = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    q = int(data[index])
    index += 1

    is_open = [[True] * (n + 1) for _ in range(2)]
    m = n - 1
    tree = [None] * (4 * (m + 2))

    if m > 0:
        build(1, 1, m, is_open, tree)

    ans = []
    for _ in range(q):
        r = int(data[index])
        index += 1
        c = int(data[index])
        index += 1
        row = r - 1
        is_open[row][c] = not is_open[row][c]
        if c > 1:
            om = (1 if is_open[0][c] else 0) | (2 if is_open[1][c] else 0)
            newf = get_transfer(om)
            pos = c - 1
            update(1, 1, m, pos, newf, tree)
        bottom1_open = is_open[1][1]
        start_state = 3 if bottom1_open else 1
        if m == 0 or tree[1] is None:
            # For n=1, but n>=2, safety
            final = start_state
        else:
            F = tree[1]
            final = F[start_state]
        if final & 2:
            ans.append("Yes")
        else:
            ans.append("No")
    print("\n".join(ans))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(400000)

def get_transfer(om):
    f = [0] * 4
    for ins in range(4):
        inc = 0
        if (ins & 1) and (om & 1):
            inc |= 1
        if (ins & 2) and (om & 2):
            inc |= 2
        out = inc
        if om == 3 and inc != 0:
            out = 3
        f[ins] = out
    return tuple(f)

def compose(g, f):
    return tuple(g[f[i]] for i in range(4))

def build(node, start, end, is_open, tree):
    if start == end:
        col = start + 1
        om = (1 if is_open[0][col] else 0) | (2 if is_open[1][col] else 0)
        tree[node] = get_transfer(om)
        return
    mid = (start + end) // 2
    build(2 * node, start, mid, is_open, tree)
    build(2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end, is_open, tree)
    tree[node] = compose(tree[2 * node + 1], tree[2 * node])

def update(node, start, end, idx, newf, tree):
    if start == end:
        tree[node] = newf
        return
    mid = (start + end) // 2
    if idx <= mid:
        update(2 * node, start, mid, idx, newf, tree)
    else:
        update(2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end, idx, newf, tree)
    tree[node] = compose(tree[2 * node + 1], tree[2 * node])

def main():
    input = sys.stdin.read
    data = input().split()
    index = 0
    n = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    q = int(data[index])
    index += 1

    is_open = [[True] * (n + 1) for _ in range(2)]
    m = n - 1
    tree = [None] * (4 * (m + 2))

    if m > 0:
        build(1, 1, m, is_open, tree)

    ans = []
    for _ in range(q):
        r = int(data[index])
        index += 1
        c = int(data[index])
        index += 1
        row = r - 1
        is_open[row][c] = not is_open[row][c]
        if c > 1:
            om = (1 if is_open[0][c] else 0) | (2 if is_open[1][c] else 0)
            newf = get_transfer(om)
            pos = c - 1
            update(1, 1, m, pos, newf, tree)
        bottom1_open = is_open[1][1]
        start_state = 3 if bottom1_open else 1
        if m == 0 or tree[1] is None:
            final = start_state
        else:
            F = tree[1]
            final = F[start_state]
        if final & 2:
            ans.append("Yes")
        else:
            ans.append("No")
    print("\n".join(ans))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(NULL);
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<int> a(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> a[i];
    }
    if (n == 0) {
        cout << 0 << endl;
        return 0;
    }
    const int LOG = 18;
    const int MAX_OR = 1 << 20;
    vector<vector<int>> st(LOG, vector<int>(n));
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        st[0][i] = a[i];
    }
    for (int k = 1; k < LOG; k++) {
        for (int i = 0; i + (1 << k) <= n; i++) {
            st[k][i] = st[k - 1][i] | st[k - 1][i + (1 << (k - 1))];
        }
    }
    vector<int> logg(n + 1, 0);
    for (int i = 2; i <= n; i++) {
        logg[i] = logg[i / 2] + 1;
    }
    auto query = [&](int L, int R) -> int {
        if (L > R) return 0;
        int len = R - L + 1;
        int k = logg[len];
        return st[k][L] | st[k][R - (1 << k) + 1];
    };
    bitset<1048576> vis;
    for (int l = 0; l < n; l++) {
        int curr_or = a[l];
        vis[curr_or] = 1;
        int r = l;
        while (r < n - 1) {
            // binary search for max rr >= r s.t. query(l, rr) == curr_or
            int low = r;
            int high = n - 1;
            int max_same = r - 1;
            while (low <= high) {
                int mid = low + (high - low) / 2;
                if (query(l, mid) == curr_or) {
                    max_same = mid;
                    low = mid + 1;
                } else {
                    high = mid - 1;
                }
            }
            if (max_same == n - 1) {
                break;
            }
            int next_r = max_same + 1;
            int new_or = query(l, next_r);
            vis[new_or] = 1;
            curr_or = new_or;
            r = next_r;
        }
    }
    cout << vis.count() << endl;
    return 0;
}
```
```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
n = int(data[0])
a = [int(x) for x in data[1:n+1]]

LOG = 18
st = [[0] * n for _ in range(LOG)]
for i in range(n):
    st[0][i] = a[i]
for k in range(1, LOG):
    for i in range(n - (1 << k) + 1):
        st[k][i] = st[k-1][i] | st[k-1][i + (1 << (k - 1))]

logg = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(2, n + 1):
    logg[i] = logg[i // 2] + 1

def query(L, R):
    if L > R:
        return 0
    length = R - L + 1
    k = logg[length]
    return st[k][L] | st[k][R - (1 << k) + 1]

vis = set()
for l in range(n):
    curr_or = a[l]
    vis.add(curr_or)
    r = l
    while r < n - 1:
        low = r
        high = n - 1
        max_same = r - 1
        while low <= high:
            mid = (low + high) // 2
            if query(l, mid) == curr_or:
                max_same = mid
                low = mid + 1
            else:
                high = mid - 1
        if max_same == n - 1:
            break
        next_r = max_same + 1
        new_or = query(l, next_r)
        vis.add(new_or)
        curr_or = new_or
        r = next_r

print(len(vis))

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
idx = 0
t = int(data[idx])
idx += 1
ms = []
for i in range(t):
    ms.append(int(data[idx]))
    idx += 1

MOD = 1000000007
answers = []
for m in ms:
    needed = set()
    stack = [m]
    while stack:
        x = stack.pop()
        if x > 0 and x not in needed:
            needed.add(x)
            q = x // 2
            for k in range(4):
                y = q - k
                if y > 0:
                    stack.append(y)
    lst = sorted(needed)
    memo = {0: 1}
    for x in lst:
        q = x // 2
        res = 0
        for k in range(4):
            yk = q - k
            res = (res + memo.get(yk, 0)) % MOD
        memo[x] = res
    answers.append(str(memo[m]))
print('\n'.join(answers))

completed 111/150, Solved: True, number of success = 25/111, acc = 22.52
```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(nullptr);
    
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    int k1;
    cin >> k1;
    vector<bool> rick(n, false);
    for (int i = 0; i < k1; i++) {
        int x;
        cin >> x;
        rick[x] = true;
    }
    int k2;
    cin >> k2;
    vector<bool> morty(n, false);
    for (int i = 0; i < k2; i++) {
        int x;
        cin >> x;
        morty[x] = true;
    }
    
    vector<int> resR(n, 0); // 0: unknown, 1: Win, 2: Lose
    vector<int> resM(n, 0);
    vector<int> countR(n, 0);
    vector<int> countM(n, 0);
    int totR = k1;
    int totM = k2;
    
    queue<int> qWinR, qWinM, qLoseR, qLoseM;
    
    for (int p = 1; p < n; p++) {
        int xreq = n - p;
        if (rick[xreq]) {
            resR[p] = 1;
            qWinR.push(p);
        } else {
            countR[p] = 0;
        }
        if (morty[xreq]) {
            resM[p] = 1;
            qWinM.push(p);
        } else {
            countM[p] = 0;
        }
    }
    
    while (!qWinR.empty() || !qWinM.empty() || !qLoseR.empty() || !qLoseM.empty()) {
        // Process qWinR: newly Win for Rick, increment countM for Morty predecessors
        while (!qWinR.empty()) {
            int p = qWinR.front();
            qWinR.pop();
            for (int x = 1; x < n; x++) {
                if (!morty[x]) continue;
                int r = (p - x + n) % n;
                if (r == 0) continue;
                if (resM[r] == 0) {
                    countM[r]++;
                    if (countM[r] == totM) {
                        resM[r] = 2;
                        qLoseM.push(r);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        // Process qWinM: newly Win for Morty, increment countR for Rick predecessors
        while (!qWinM.empty()) {
            int q = qWinM.front();
            qWinM.pop();
            for (int x = 1; x < n; x++) {
                if (!rick[x]) continue;
                int p = (q - x + n) % n;
                if (p == 0) continue;
                if (resR[p] == 0) {
                    countR[p]++;
                    if (countR[p] == totR) {
                        resR[p] = 2;
                        qLoseR.push(p);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        // Process qLoseR: newly Lose for Rick, mark Win for Morty predecessors
        while (!qLoseR.empty()) {
            int p = qLoseR.front();
            qLoseR.pop();
            for (int x = 1; x < n; x++) {
                if (!morty[x]) continue;
                int r = (p - x + n) % n;
                if (r == 0) continue;
                if (resM[r] == 0) {
                    resM[r] = 1;
                    qWinM.push(r);
                }
            }
        }
        // Process qLoseM: newly Lose for Morty, mark Win for Rick predecessors
        while (!qLoseM.empty()) {
            int q = qLoseM.front();
            qLoseM.pop();
            for (int x = 1; x < n; x++) {
                if (!rick[x]) continue;
                int p = (q - x + n) % n;
                if (p == 0) continue;
                if (resR[p] == 0) {
                    resR[p] = 1;
                    qWinR.push(p);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Output first line: Rick first
    for (int p = 1; p < n; p++) {
        string s;
        if (resR[p] == 1) s = "Win";
        else if (resR[p] == 2) s = "Lose";
        else s = "Loop";
        cout << s;
        if (p < n - 1) cout << " ";
        else cout << "\n";
    }
    // Output second line: Morty first
    for (int p = 1; p < n; p++) {
        string s;
        if (resM[p] == 1) s = "Win";
        else if (resM[p] == 2) s = "Lose";
        else s = "Loop";
        cout << s;
        if (p < n - 1) cout << " ";
        else cout << "\n";
    }
    
    return 0;
}

```python
import sys
from collections import deque

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

idx = 0
n = int(data[idx])
idx += 1
k1 = int(data[idx])
idx += 1
rick_moves = []
for _ in range(k1):
    x = int(data[idx])
    idx += 1
    rick_moves.append(x)
k2 = int(data[idx])
idx += 1
morty_moves = []
for _ in range(k2):
    x = int(data[idx])
    idx += 1
    morty_moves.append(x)

rick_set = set(rick_moves)
morty_set = set(morty_moves)
totR = k1
totM = k2

resR = [0] * n
resM = [0] * n
countR = [0] * n
countM = [0] * n

qWinR = deque()
qWinM = deque()
qLoseR = deque()
qLoseM = deque()

for p in range(1, n):
    xreq = n - p
    if xreq in rick_set:
        resR[p] = 1
        qWinR.append(p)
    if xreq in morty_set:
        resM[p] = 1
        qWinM.append(p)

while qWinR or qWinM or qLoseR or qLoseM:
    while qWinR:
        p = qWinR.popleft()
        for x in morty_moves:
            r = (p - x + n) % n
            if r == 0:
                continue
            if resM[r] == 0:
                countM[r] += 1
                if countM[r] == totM:
                    resM[r] = 2
                    qLoseM.append(r)
    while qWinM:
        q_ = qWinM.popleft()
        for x in rick_moves:
            p = (q_ - x + n) % n
            if p == 0:
                continue
            if resR[p] == 0:
                countR[p] += 1
                if countR[p] == totR:
                    resR[p] = 2
                    qLoseR.append(p)
    while qLoseR:
        p = qLoseR.popleft()
        for x in morty_moves:
            r = (p - x + n) % n
            if r == 0:
                continue
            if resM[r] == 0:
                resM[r] = 1
                qWinM.append(r)
    while qLoseM:
        q_ = qLoseM.popleft()
        for x in rick_moves:
            p = (q_ - x + n) % n
            if p == 0:
                continue
            if resR[p] == 0:
                resR[p] = 1
                qWinR.append(p)

line1 = []
for p in range(1, n):
    if resR[p] == 1:
        line1.append("Win")
    elif resR[p] == 2:
        line1.append("Lose")
    else:
        line1.append("Loop")
print(" ".join(line1))

line2 = []
for p in range(1, n):
    if resM[p] == 1:
        line2.append("Win")
    elif resM[p] == 2:
        line2.append("Lose")
    else:
        line2.append("Loop")
print(" ".join(line2))

completed 113/150, Solved: True, number of success = 27/113, acc = 23.89
```python
import sys
from collections import defaultdict

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
q = int(data[index])
index += 1

a = []
for i in range(n):
    a.append(int(data[index]))
    index += 1

cnt = defaultdict(int)
first_pos = {}
last_pos = {}

for i in range(n):
    val = a[i]
    cnt[val] += 1
    if val not in first_pos:
        first_pos[val] = i + 1
    last_pos[val] = i + 1

intervals = []
for val in cnt:
    L = first_pos[val]
    R = last_pos[val]
    f = cnt[val]
    intervals.append((L, R, f))

intervals.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])

unchanged = 0
if intervals:
    cur_max_f = 0
    cur_max_r = -1
    for L, R, f in intervals:
        if L > cur_max_r:
            unchanged += cur_max_f
            cur_max_f = f
            cur_max_r = R
        else:
            cur_max_f = max(cur_max_f, f)
            cur_max_r = max(cur_max_r, R)
    unchanged += cur_max_f

difficulty = n - unchanged
print(difficulty)
```

        first_pos[val] = i + 1
    last_pos[val] = i + 1

for val in cnt:
    L = first_pos[val]
    R = last_pos[val]
    f = cnt[val]
    intervals.append((L, R, f))

if intervals:
    cur_max_f = 0
    cur_max_r = -1
    for L, R, f in intervals:
        if L > cur_max_r:
            unchanged += cur_max_f

            cur_max_r = R

            cur_max_f = max(cur_max_f, f)

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
t = int(data[index])
index += 1
MOD = 10**9 + 7

for _ in range(t):
    x = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    s = data[index]
    index += 1
    n = len(s)
    chars = list(s[:x])
    L_mod = n % MOD
    for ell in range(1, x + 1):
        k = int(chars[ell - 1])
        c_len_mod = (L_mod + MOD - ell) % MOD
        L_mod = (ell + (k * c_len_mod) % MOD) % MOD
        if len(chars) < x and k > 1:
            suffix_start = ell
            suffix_end = len(chars)
            num_copies = k - 1
            for __ in range(num_copies):
                for j in range(suffix_start, suffix_end):
                    chars.append(chars[j])
            if len(chars) > x:
                chars = chars[:x]
    print(L_mod)

s = input().strip()
n = len(s)
prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == 'Q' else 0)
ans = 0
for j in range(n):

        left = prefix[j]
        right = prefix[n] - prefix[j + 1]

```python
import sys

class SegTree:
    def __init__(self, n):
        self.n = n
        self.tree = [0] * (4 * n)

    def update(self, idx, val):
        self._update(0, 0, self.n - 1, idx, val)

    def _update(self, node, l, r, idx, val):
        if l == r:
            self.tree[node] = val
            return
        m = (l + r) // 2
        if idx <= m:
            self._update(2 * node + 1, l, m, idx, val)
        else:
            self._update(2 * node + 2, m + 1, r, idx, val)
        self.tree[node] = max(self.tree[2 * node + 1], self.tree[2 * node + 2])

    def query(self, ql, qr):
        if ql > qr:
            return 0
        return self._query(0, 0, self.n - 1, ql, qr)

    def _query(self, node, l, r, ql, qr):
        if ql <= l and r <= qr:
            return self.tree[node]
        if r < ql or l > qr:
            return 0
        m = (l + r) // 2
        return max(self._query(2 * node + 1, l, m, ql, qr), self._query(2 * node + 2, m + 1, r, ql, qr))

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()
index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
a = [int(data[index + i]) for i in range(n)]
INF = n + 2
dp = [0] * n
seg = SegTree(n)
ans = 0
stack = []
dp[0] = INF
seg.update(0, INF)
stack.append(0)
for i in range(1, n):
    while stack and a[stack[-1]] <= a[i]:
        stack.pop()
    j = stack[-1] if stack else -1
    if j == -1:
        dp[i] = INF
    else:
        l = j + 1
        r = i - 1
        mx = seg.query(l, r)
        dp[i] = 1 + mx
    if dp[i] < INF:
        ans = max(ans, dp[i])
    seg.update(i, dp[i])
    stack.append(i)
print(ans)
```
```python
import sys

class SegTree:
    def __init__(self, n):
        self.n = n
        self.tree = [0] * (4 * n)

    def update(self, idx, val):
        self._update(0, 0, self.n - 1, idx, val)

    def _update(self, node, l, r, idx, val):
        if l == r:
            self.tree[node] = val
            return
        m = (l + r) // 2
        if idx <= m:
            self._update(2 * node + 1, l, m, idx, val)
        else:
            self._update(2 * node + 2, m + 1, r, idx, val)
        self.tree[node] = max(self.tree[2 * node + 1], self.tree[2 * node + 2])

    def query(self, ql, qr):
        if ql > qr:
            return 0
        return self._query(0, 0, self.n - 1, ql, qr)

    def _query(self, node, l, r, ql, qr):
        if ql <= l and r <= qr:
            return self.tree[node]
        if r < ql or l > qr:
            return 0
        m = (l + r) // 2
        return max(self._query(2 * node + 1, l, m, ql, qr), self._query(2 * node + 2, m + 1, r, ql, qr))

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
a = [int(data[index + i]) for i in range(n)]
INF = n + 2
dp = [0] * n
seg = SegTree(n)
ans = 0
stack = []
dp[0] = INF
seg.update(0, INF)
stack.append(0)
for i in range(1, n):
    while stack and a[stack[-1]] <= a[i]:
        stack.pop()
    j = stack[-1] if stack else -1
    if j == -1:
        dp[i] = INF
    else:
        l = j + 1
        r = i - 1
        mx = seg.query(l, r)
        dp[i] = 1 + mx

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
n = int(data[0])
a = [0] + [int(x) for x in data[1:]]
color = [0] * (n + 1)
cycles = []
reps = []
singletons = []

for i in range(1, n + 1):
    if color[i] == 0:
        path = []
        cur = i
        while color[cur] == 0:
            color[cur] = 1
            path.append(cur)
            cur = a[cur]
        if color[cur] == 1:
            try:
                start = path.index(cur)
                cycle = path[start:]
                cycles.append(cycle)
                rep = min(cycle)
                reps.append(rep)
                if len(cycle) == 1:
                    singletons.append(rep)
            except ValueError:
                pass
        for node in path:
            color[node] = 2

C = len(cycles)
K = len(singletons)
min_changes = C - 1 if K > 0 else C

p = a[:]

if K > 0:
    r = max(singletons)
    for j in range(C):
        if reps[j] != r:
            p[reps[j]] = r
else:
    if C > 0:
        idx_root = 0
        max_rep = -1
        for i in range(C):
            if reps[i] > max_rep:
                max_rep = reps[i]
                idx_root = i
        root_cycle = cycles[idx_root]
        r = max(root_cycle)
        p[r] = r
        for i in range(C):
            if i != idx_root:
                p[reps[i]] = r

print(min_changes)
print(' '.join(map(str, p[1:])))
```
```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
n = int(data[0])
a = [0] + [int(x) for x in data[1:]]
color = [0] * (n + 1)
cycles = []
reps = []
singletons = []

for i in range(1, n + 1):
    if color[i] == 0:
        path = []
        cur = i
        while color[cur] == 0:
            color[cur] = 1
            path.append(cur)
            cur = a[cur]
        if color[cur] == 1:
            try:
                start = path.index(cur)
                cycle = path[start:]
                cycles.append(cycle)
                rep = min(cycle)
                reps.append(rep)
                if len(cycle) == 1:
                    singletons.append(rep)
            except ValueError:
                pass
        for node in path:
            color[node] = 2

C = len(cycles)
K = len(singletons)
min_changes = C - 1 if K > 0 else C

p = a[:]

if K > 0:
    r = max(singletons)
    for j in range(C):
        if reps[j] != r:
            p[reps[j]] = r
else:
    if C > 0:
        idx_root = 0
        max_rep = -1
        for i in range(C):
            if reps[i] > max_rep:
                max_rep = reps[i]
                idx_root = i
        root_cycle = cycles[idx_root]
        r = max(root_cycle)
        p[r] = r
        for i in range(C):
            if i != idx_root:
                p[reps[i]] = r

print(min_changes)
print(' '.join(map(str, p[1:])))

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index]); index += 1
a = int(data[index]); index += 1
b = int(data[index]); index += 1
T = int(data[index]); index += 1
s = data[index]

cost = [0] * n
for i in range(n):
    cost[i] = 1
    if s[i] == 'w':
        cost[i] += b

right_sum = [0] * (n + 1)
for r in range(1, n):
    right_sum[r] = right_sum[r - 1] + cost[r]

left_sum = [0] * (n + 1)
for m in range(1, n):
    idx = n - m
    left_sum[m] = left_sum[m - 1] + cost[idx]

def possible(kk):
    if kk == 0:
        return True
    d = kk - 1
    c0 = cost[0]
    for m in range(d + 1):
        r = d - m
        sumc = c0 + left_sum[m] + right_sum[r]
        moves1 = 2 * m + r
        moves2 = 2 * r + m
        numm = min(moves1, moves2)
        timet = sumc + numm * a
        if timet <= T:
            return True
    return False

lo = 0
hi = n
while lo < hi:
    mid = (lo + hi + 1) // 2
    if possible(mid):
        lo = mid
    else:
        hi = mid - 1

print(lo)
```
```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index]); index += 1
a = int(data[index]); index += 1
b = int(data[index]); index += 1
T = int(data[index]); index += 1
s = data[index]

cost = [0] * n
for i in range(n):
    cost[i] = 1
    if s[i] == 'w':
        cost[i] += b

right_sum = [0] * (n + 1)
for r in range(1, n):
    right_sum[r] = right_sum[r - 1] + cost[r]

left_sum = [0] * (n + 1)
for m in range(1, n):
    idx = n - m
    left_sum[m] = left_sum[m - 1] + cost[idx]

def possible(kk):
    if kk == 0:
        return True
    d = kk - 1
    c0 = cost[0]
    for m in range(d + 1):
        r = d - m
        sumc = c0 + left_sum[m] + right_sum[r]
        moves1 = 2 * m + r
        moves2 = 2 * r + m
        numm = min(moves1, moves2)
        timet = sumc + numm * a
        if timet <= T:
            return True
    return False

lo = 0
hi = n
while lo < hi:
    mid = (lo + hi + 1) // 2
    if possible(mid):
        lo = mid
    else:
        hi = mid - 1

print(lo)
```
completed 119/150, Solved: True, number of success = 32/119, acc = 26.89
```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

using ll = long long;

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(nullptr);

    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<int> A(n), B(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> A[i] >> B[i];
    }

    // Precompute consec
    vector<vector<int>> consec(10, vector<int>(n + 1, 0));
    for (int start = n - 1; start >= 0; start--) {
        int f = A[start];
        consec[f][start] = 1 + (start + 1 < n ? consec[f][start + 1] : 0);
    }

    // Generate configs
    vector<array<int, 10>> configs;
    vector<int> code_to_id(1953125, -1);
    vector<int> occupancy;
    array<int, 10> cur{};
    function<void(int, int)> gen = [&](int fl, int rem_slots) {
        if (fl == 10) {
            int code = 0;
            int base = 1;
            int tot = 0;
            for (int f = 1; f <= 9; f++) {
                code += cur[f] * base;
                tot += cur[f];
                base *= 5;
            }
            int cid = configs.size();
            configs.push_back(cur);
            code_to_id[code] = cid;
            occupancy.push_back(tot);
            return;
        }
        for (int cnt = 0; cnt <= rem_slots; cnt++) {
            cur[fl] = cnt;
            gen(fl + 1, rem_slots - cnt);
        }
    };
    gen(1, 4);

    int NCID = configs.size();
    int empty_cid = code_to_id[0];

    // dist
    int NPOS = 10;
    int NNXT = n + 1;
    vector<ll> dist_vec(NPOS * NNXT * NCID, 1LL << 60);
    auto idx = [&](int p, int nx, int ci) -> int {
        return ((p * NNXT + nx) * NCID + ci);
    };

    // dijkstra
    using T = tuple<ll, int, int, int>; // cost, pos, nxt, cid
    priority_queue<T, vector<T>, greater<T>> pq;
    dist_vec[idx(1, 0, empty_cid)] = 0;
    pq.emplace(0, 1, 0, empty_cid);

    while (!pq.empty()) {
        auto [cost, pos, nxt, cid] = pq.top();
        pq.pop();
        int idxx = idx(pos, nxt, cid);
        if (cost > dist_vec[idxx]) continue;

        // move up
        if (pos < 9) {
            int np = pos + 1;
            ll nc = cost + 1;
            int inx = idx(np, nxt, cid);
            if (nc < dist_vec[inx]) {
                dist_vec[inx] = nc;
                pq.emplace(nc, np, nxt, cid);
            }
        }
        // move down
        if (pos > 1) {
            int np = pos - 1;
            ll nc = cost + 1;
            int inx = idx(np, nxt, cid);
            if (nc < dist_vec[inx]) {
                dist_vec[inx] = nc;
                pq.emplace(nc, np, nxt, cid);
            }
        }
        // open
        {
            array<int, 10> conf = configs[cid];
            int d = conf[pos];
            int total_old = occupancy[cid];
            int new_total_after_drop = total_old - d;
            int avail = 4 - new_total_after_drop;
            int f = pos;
            int maxp = (nxt < n ? consec[f][nxt] : 0);
            int p = min(avail, maxp);
            int new_nxt = nxt + p;
            array<int, 10> new_conf = conf;
            new_conf[pos] = 0;
            for (int i = 0; i < p; i++) {
                int person = nxt + i;
                int destt = B[person];
                new_conf[destt]++;
            }
            int new_code = 0;
            int basee = 1;
            for (int ff = 1; ff <= 9; ff++) {
                new_code += new_conf[ff] * basee;
                basee *= 5;
            }
            int new_cid = code_to_id[new_code];
            ll addt = (ll)d + p;
            ll nc = cost + addt;
            int npos = pos;
            int inx = idx(npos, new_nxt, new_cid);
            if (nc < dist_vec[inx]) {
                dist_vec[inx] = nc;
                pq.emplace(nc, npos, new_nxt, new_cid);
            }
        }
    }

    ll ans = 1LL << 60;
    for (int p = 1; p <= 9; p++) {
        ans = min(ans, dist_vec[idx(p, n, empty_cid)]);
    }
    if (ans == (1LL << 60)) {
        cout << -1 << '\n';
    } else {
        cout << ans << '\n';
    }

    return 0;
}
```

## Explanation

The provided code solves the elevator management problem using dynamic programming with Dijkstra's algorithm to find the minimum time required to deliver all employees.

**Key Insights:**
- Employees must enter the elevator in the given order, which enforces a strict sequence for pickups.
- The elevator's state is defined by: current position (1-9), next employee to pick up (0 to n), and the configuration of passengers inside (counts of passengers destined for each floor 1-9, with total ≤4).
- There are 9 positions, n+1 next values (up to 2001), and approximately 715 possible configurations (non-negative integers summing to ≤4 across 9 floors), yielding ~12.8 million states.

**Precomputations:**
- **Consecutive pickups (`consec`)**: For each starting employee index and floor, precompute the length of consecutive employees waiting at that floor. This allows O(1) computation of pickups during door opens.
- **Configurations**: Recursively generate all valid elevator configurations (counts per destination summing to ≤4). Encode each as a base-5 integer (0 to ~2M) for fast lookup via `code_to_id`. Store in `configs` and precompute occupancy.

**State Representation:**
- State encoded as (position, next_employee, config_id).
- Distance array `dist_vec` stores minimum time to reach each state, accessed via flat index.

**Dijkstra's Algorithm:**
- **Priority queue** processes states by increasing time cost.
- **Transitions**:
  - **Move up/down**: +1 second to adjacent floor, same next and config.
  - **Open doors** at current position:
    - Drop all passengers destined here (d = config[pos], +d seconds).
    - Compute available space (4 - (occupancy - d)).
    - Pickup p = min(available, consecutive at this floor from next).
    - Update config: zero out pos count, increment dest counts for picked employees.
    - Advance next by p, +p seconds.
- Ensures all mandatory pickups (as many as possible) occur during opens.

**Final Answer:**
- Minimum time over all positions where next == n and elevator is empty (config_id of all-zero).

This approach handles capacity constraints, entry order, and optimal routing/dropping, matching sample outputs (10 and 12 seconds).
```python
import sys
import heapq

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
A = [0] * n
B = [0] * n
for i in range(n):
    A[i] = int(data[index])
    B[i] = int(data[index + 1])
    index += 2

cur = [0] * 10
configs = []
code_to_id = [-1] * 1953125
occupancy = []

def gen(fl, rem):
    if fl == 10:
        code = 0
        base = 1
        tot = 0
        for f in range(1, 10):
            code += cur[f] * base
            tot += cur[f]
            base *= 5
        cid = len(configs)
        configs.append(cur[:])
        code_to_id[code] = cid
        occupancy.append(tot)
        return
    for cnt in range(rem + 1):
        cur[fl] = cnt
        gen(fl + 1, rem - cnt)

gen(1, 4)

NCID = len(configs)
empty_cid = code_to_id[0]

consec = [[0] * (n + 1) for _ in range(10)]
for start in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    f = A[start]
    consec[f][start] = 1 + (consec[f][start + 1] if start + 1 < n else 0)

NPOS = 10
NNXT = n + 1
INF = 1 << 60
dist_vec = [INF] * (NPOS * NNXT * NCID)

def idx(p, nx, ci):
    return ((p * NNXT + nx) * NCID + ci)

pq = []
state0 = idx(1, 0, empty_cid)
dist_vec[state0] = 0
heapq.heappush(pq, (0, 1, 0, empty_cid))

while pq:
    cost, pos, nxt, cid = heapq.heappop(pq)
    idxx = idx(pos, nxt, cid)
    if cost > dist_vec[idxx]:
        continue
    # up
    if pos < 9:
        np = pos + 1
        nc = cost + 1
        inx = idx(np, nxt, cid)
        if nc < dist_vec[inx]:
            dist_vec[inx] = nc
            heapq.heappush(pq, (nc, np, nxt, cid))
    # down
    if pos > 1:
        np = pos - 1
        nc = cost + 1
        inx = idx(np, nxt, cid)
        if nc < dist_vec[inx]:
            dist_vec[inx] = nc
            heapq.heappush(pq, (nc, np, nxt, cid))
    # open
    conf = configs[cid]
    d = conf[pos]
    total_old = occupancy[cid]
    new_total_after_drop = total_old - d
    avail = 4 - new_total_after_drop
    f = pos
    maxp = consec[f][nxt] if nxt < n else 0
    p = min(avail, maxp)
    new_nxt = nxt + p
    new_conf = conf[:]
    new_conf[pos] = 0
    for i in range(p):
        person = nxt + i
        destt = B[person]
        new_conf[destt] += 1
    new_code = 0
    base = 1
    for ff in range(1, 10):
        new_code += new_conf[ff] * base
        base *= 5
    new_cid = code_to_id[new_code]
    addt = d + p
    nc = cost + addt
    npos = pos
    inx = idx(npos, new_nxt, new_cid)
    if nc < dist_vec[inx]:
        dist_vec[inx] = nc
        heapq.heappush(pq, (nc, npos, new_nxt, new_cid))

ans = INF
for p in range(1, 10):
    i = idx(p, n, empty_cid)
    if dist_vec[i] < ans:
        ans = dist_vec[i]
print(ans if ans < INF else -1)
```
completed 120/150, Solved: True, number of success = 33/120, acc = 27.5
```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().strip()
s = data
n = len(s)

prefix_open = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix_open[i + 1] = prefix_open[i] or (s[i] == '[')

suffix_close = [False] * (n + 1)
suffix_close[n] = False
for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
    suffix_close[i] = suffix_close[i + 1] or (s[i] == ']')

pipe = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    pipe[i + 1] = pipe[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

INF = n + 1
min_after = INF
max_count = -1

for t in range(n):
    # First, check if valid second colon
    if s[t] == ':' and suffix_close[t + 1]:
        if min_after < INF:
            cnt = pipe[t] - min_after
            if cnt > max_count:
                max_count = cnt
    # Then, update if valid first colon
    if s[t] == ':' and prefix_open[t]:
        min_after = min(min_after, pipe[t + 1])

if max_count == -1:
    print(-1)
else:
    print(max_count + 4)
```
```python
import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(200010)
input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index]); index += 1
k = int(data[index]); index += 1

adj = [[] for _ in range(n + 1)]
for _ in range(n - 1):
    u = int(data[index]); index += 1
    v = int(data[index]); index += 1
    adj[u].append(v)
    adj[v].append(u)

depth = [0] * (n + 1)
sz = [0] * (n + 1)

def dfs1(u, p):
    sz[u] = 1
    depth[u] = depth[p] + 1 if u != 1 else 0
    for v in adj[u]:
        if v != p:
            dfs1(v, u)
            sz[u] += sz[v]

dfs1(1, 0)

nodes = []
for u in range(1, n + 1):
    nodes.append((-depth[u], sz[u], u))

nodes.sort()

sum_depth = 0
is_ind = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(k):
    u = nodes[i][2]
    is_ind[u] = True
    sum_depth += depth[u]

desc_ind = [0] * (n + 1)

def dfs2(u, p):
    res = 1 if is_ind[u] else 0
    for v in adj[u]:
        if v != p:
            res += dfs2(v, u)
    desc_ind[u] = res
    return res

dfs2(1, 0)

total_pairs = 0
for u in range(1, n + 1):
    if is_ind[u]:
        total_pairs += desc_ind[u] - 1

ans = sum_depth - total_pairs
print(ans)
```

```python
import sys
from collections import deque

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
idx = 0
k = int(data[idx])
idx += 1

box_lists = [[] for _ in range(k)]
S = [0] * k
num_to_box = {}
for i in range(k):
    ni = int(data[idx])
    idx += 1
    for _ in range(ni):
        a = int(data[idx])
        idx += 1
        box_lists[i].append(a)
        if a in num_to_box:
            pass  # guaranteed distinct
        num_to_box[a] = i
        S[i] += a

total = sum(S)
if k == 0 or total % k != 0:
    print("No")
    sys.exit(0)

T = total // k
delta = [T - S[i] for i in range(k)]

full = (1 << k) - 1
can_cycle = [False] * (1 << k)
cycle_assign = {}

for i in range(k):
    for c in box_lists[i]:
        visited_mask = 1 << i
        box_to_num = {i: c}
        curr_num = c
        curr_box = i
        success = False
        for _ in range(k):
            next_num = curr_num + delta[curr_box]
            if next_num not in num_to_box:
                break
            next_box = num_to_box[next_num]
            if (visited_mask & (1 << next_box)) != 0:
                if next_box == i and next_num == c:
                    success = True
                break
            visited_mask |= (1 << next_box)
            box_to_num[next_box] = next_num
            curr_num = next_num
            curr_box = next_box
        if success:
            S_mask = visited_mask
            can_cycle[S_mask] = True
            if S_mask not in cycle_assign:
                cycle_assign[S_mask] = box_to_num.copy()

dp = [False] * (1 << k)
dp[0] = True
for mask in range(1 << k):
    if not dp[mask]:
        continue
    rem = full ^ mask
    sub = rem
    while True:
        if can_cycle[sub]:
            dp[mask | sub] = True
        if sub == 0:
            break
        sub = (sub - 1) & rem

if not dp[full]:
    print("No")
else:
    # reconstruct
    chosen_c = [0] * k
    current = full
    cycle_list = list(cycle_assign.keys())
    while current != 0:
        found = False
        for T in cycle_list:
            if (T & current) == T and dp[current ^ T]:
                assign = cycle_assign[T]
                for bx, numm in assign.items():
                    chosen_c[bx] = numm
                current ^= T
                found = True
                break
        assert found
    # compute received_to_box
    received_to_box = {}
    for j in range(k):
        pj = chosen_c[j] + delta[j]
        received_to_box[pj] = j
    print("Yes")
    for i in range(k):
        ci = chosen_c[i]
        pi = received_to_box[ci] + 1
        print(ci, pi)
```

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)

prefix_open = [0] * (n + 1)
prefix_close = [0] * (n + 1)
prefix_pipe = [0] * (n + 1)

for i in range(n):
    prefix_open[i + 1] = prefix_open[i] + (1 if data[i] == '[' else 0)
    prefix_close[i + 1] = prefix_close[i] + (1 if data[i] == ']' else 0)
    prefix_pipe[i + 1] = prefix_pipe[i] + (1 if data[i] == '|' else 0)

total_close = prefix_close[n]

min_prefix = 10**9  # larger than n=5e5
max_diff = -1

for i in range(n):
    # Check if can be second colon (j)
    if data[i] == ':' and total_close - prefix_close[i + 1] >= 1:
        if min_prefix < 10**9:
            diff = prefix_pipe[i] - min_prefix
            if diff > max_diff:
                max_diff = diff
    # Then add as possible first colon (i for future j)
    if data[i] == ':' and prefix_open[i] >= 1:
        if prefix_pipe[i] < min_prefix:
            min_prefix = prefix_pipe[i]

if max_diff == -1:
    print(-1)
else:
    print(4 + max_diff)
```
```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
n = int(data[0])
a = list(map(int, data[1:]))
MOD = 10**9 + 7
N = n - 1
g = N // 4
h = 2 * g
rem = N % 4
is_odd_n = (n % 2 == 1)

# Compute r coeffs
r = [0] * (rem + 1)
if rem == 0:
    r[0] = 1
elif rem == 1:
    r[0] = 1
    r[1] = 1
elif rem == 2:
    if is_odd_n:
        r[0] = 1
        r[1] = 2
        r[2] = 1
    else:
        r[0] = 1
        r[1] = 0
        r[2] = MOD - 1
elif rem == 3:
    if is_odd_n:
        r[0] = 1
        r[1] = 1
        r[2] = MOD - 1
        r[3] = MOD - 1
    else:
        r[0] = 1
        r[1] = MOD - 1
        r[2] = MOD - 1
        r[3] = 1

# Precompute fact and invfact
MAXN = 200010
fact = [0] * MAXN
fact[0] = 1
for i in range(1, MAXN):
    fact[i] = fact[i - 1] * i % MOD
invfact = [0] * MAXN
invfact[MAXN - 1] = pow(fact[MAXN - 1], MOD - 2, MOD)
for i in range(MAXN - 2, -1, -1):
    invfact[i] = invfact[i + 1] * (i + 1) % MOD

def binom(nn, kk):
    if kk < 0 or kk > nn:
        return 0
    return fact[nn] * invfact[kk] % MOD * invfact[nn - kk] % MOD

# Compute e
e = [0] * (N + 1)
for k in range(N + 1):
    for l in range(rem + 1):
        rl = r[l]
        if rl == 0:
            continue
        dd = k - l
        if dd >= 0 and dd % 2 == 0:
            m = dd // 2
            if 0 <= m <= h:
                b = binom(h, m)
                sgn = 1 if m % 2 == 0 else MOD - 1
                contrib = rl * b % MOD * sgn % MOD
                e[k] = (e[k] + contrib) % MOD

# Compute ans
ans = 0
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    k = i - 1
    if k % 4 == 0 or k % 4 == 1:
        sg = 1
    else:
        sg = MOD - 1
    coeff = sg * e[k] % MOD
    ans = (ans + coeff * a[i - 1] % MOD) % MOD

print(ans)
```

```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
using ll = long long;
int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(0);
    int n, m, k;
    cin >> n >> m >> k;
    vector<vector<pair<int, ll>>> g(n + 1);
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
        int u, v;
        ll x;
        cin >> u >> v >> x;
        g[u].emplace_back(v, x);
        g[v].emplace_back(u, x);
    }
    const ll INF = LLONG_MAX / 2;
    vector<ll> road_dist(n + 1, INF);
    road_dist[1] = 0;
    priority_queue<pair<ll, int>, vector<pair<ll, int>>, greater<pair<ll, int>>> pq;
    pq.push({0, 1});
    while (!pq.empty()) {
        auto [d, u] = pq.top();
        pq.pop();
        if (d > road_dist[u]) continue;
        for (auto [v, w] : g[u]) {
            if (road_dist[v] > road_dist[u] + w) {
                road_dist[v] = road_dist[u] + w;
                pq.push({road_dist[v], v});
            }
        }
    }
    vector<pair<int, ll>> trains;
    trains.reserve(k);
    vector<ll> dist(n + 1, INF);
    priority_queue<pair<ll, int>, vector<pair<ll, int>>, greater<pair<ll, int>>> pq2;
    dist[1] = 0;
    pq2.push({0, 1});
    for (int i = 0; i < k; i++) {
        int s;
        ll y;
        cin >> s >> y;
        trains.emplace_back(s, y);
        if (y < dist[s]) {
            dist[s] = y;
            pq2.push({y, s});
        }
    }
    while (!pq2.empty()) {
        auto [d, u] = pq2.top();
        pq2.pop();
        if (d > dist[u]) continue;
        for (auto [v, w] : g[u]) {
            if (dist[v] > dist[u] + w) {
                dist[v] = dist[u] + w;
                pq2.push({dist[v], v});
            }
        }
    }
    vector<bool> has_rel(n + 1, false);
    for (auto [s, y] : trains) {
        if (dist[s] != INF && y == dist[s]) {
            has_rel[s] = true;
        }
    }
    vector<int> sources;
    for (int i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
        if (has_rel[i]) sources.push_back(i);
    }
    vector<ll> portal(n + 1, INF);
    priority_queue<pair<ll, int>, vector<pair<ll, int>>, greater<pair<ll, int>>> pq3;
    for (int t : sources) {
        portal[t] = dist[t];
        pq3.push({portal[t], t});
    }
    while (!pq3.empty()) {
        auto [d, u] = pq3.top();
        pq3.pop();
        if (d > portal[u]) continue;
        for (auto [v, w] : g[u]) {
            if (portal[v] > portal[u] + w) {
                portal[v] = portal[u] + w;
                pq3.push({portal[v], v});
            }
        }
    }
    int num_keep = 0;
    for (int c : sources) {
        bool covered_by_road = (road_dist[c] == dist[c]);
        bool covered_by_portal = false;
        for (auto [u, w] : g[c]) {
            if (portal[u] != INF && portal[u] + w == dist[c]) {
                covered_by_portal = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!covered_by_road && !covered_by_portal) {
            num_keep++;
        }
    }
    cout << k - num_keep << '\n';
}

```python
import sys
import heapq

INF = 10**20

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
idx = 0
n = int(data[idx]); idx += 1
m = int(data[idx]); idx += 1
k = int(data[idx]); idx += 1

g = [[] for _ in range(n + 1)]
for _ in range(m):
    u = int(data[idx]); idx += 1
    v = int(data[idx]); idx += 1
    x = int(data[idx]); idx += 1
    g[u].append((v, x))
    g[v].append((u, x))

# Compute road_dist
road_dist = [INF] * (n + 1)
road_dist[1] = 0
pq = []
heapq.heappush(pq, (0, 1))
while pq:
    d, u = heapq.heappop(pq)
    if d > road_dist[u]:
        continue
    for v, w in g[u]:
        if road_dist[v] > road_dist[u] + w:
            road_dist[v] = road_dist[u] + w
            heapq.heappush(pq, (road_dist[v], v))

# Compute dist with trains
dist = [INF] * (n + 1)
dist[1] = 0
pq = []
heapq.heappush(pq, (0, 1))
trains = []
for _ in range(k):
    s = int(data[idx]); idx += 1
    y = int(data[idx]); idx += 1
    trains.append((s, y))
    if y < dist[s]:
        dist[s] = y
        heapq.heappush(pq, (y, s))
while pq:
    d, u = heapq.heappop(pq)
    if d > dist[u]:
        continue
    for v, w in g[u]:
        if dist[v] > dist[u] + w:
            dist[v] = dist[u] + w
            heapq.heappush(pq, (dist[v], v))

# Find sources (cities with tight trains)
has_rel = [False] * (n + 1)
for s, y in trains:
    if dist[s] != INF and y == dist[s]:
        has_rel[s] = True
sources = [i for i in range(1, n + 1) if has_rel[i]]

# Compute portal
portal = [INF] * (n + 1)
pq = []
for t in sources:
    portal[t] = dist[t]
    heapq.heappush(pq, (portal[t], t))
while pq:
    d, u = heapq.heappop(pq)
    if d > portal[u]:
        continue
    for v, w in g[u]:
        if portal[v] > portal[u] + w:
            portal[v] = portal[u] + w
            heapq.heappush(pq, (portal[v], v))

# Count necessary keeps
num_keep = 0
for c in sources:
    covered_by_road = (road_dist[c] == dist[c])
    covered_by_portal = False
    for u, w in g[c]:
        if portal[u] != INF and portal[u] + w == dist[c]:
            covered_by_portal = True
            break
    if not covered_by_road and not covered_by_portal:
        num_keep += 1

print(k - num_keep)

```python
import sys
import math

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()
n = int(data[0])

if n < 2:
    print(0)
    sys.exit(0)

# Sieve to find primes
is_prime = [True] * (n + 1)
is_prime[0] = is_prime[1] = False
for i in range(2, int(math.sqrt(n)) + 1):
    if is_prime[i]:
        for j in range(i * i, n + 1, i):
            is_prime[j] = False

m = n // 2

# Collect even and odd candidates
evens = []
odds = []
for i in range(2, n + 1):
    if is_prime[i] and i > m:
        continue
    if i % 2 == 0:
        evens.append(i)
    else:
        odds.append(i)

used = [False] * (n + 1)
pairs = []

ptr_e = 0
ptr_o = 0

while ptr_e < len(evens) or ptr_o < len(odds):
    if ptr_e >= len(evens):
        i = odds[ptr_o]
        ptr_o += 1
        i_parity = 1
    elif ptr_o >= len(odds):
        i = evens[ptr_e]
        ptr_e += 1
        i_parity = 0
    else:
        if evens[ptr_e] < odds[ptr_o]:
            i = evens[ptr_e]
            ptr_e += 1
            i_parity = 0
        else:
            i = odds[ptr_o]
            ptr_o += 1
            i_parity = 1

    if used[i]:
        continue

    found = False

    # Same parity first
    if i_parity == 0:
        # even, same even
        k = ptr_e
        while k < len(evens):
            j = evens[k]
            if not used[j]:
                pairs.append((i, j))
                used[j] = True
                found = True
                break
            k += 1
    else:
        # odd, same odd
        k = ptr_o
        while k < len(odds):
            j = odds[k]
            if not used[j] and math.gcd(i, j) > 1:
                pairs.append((i, j))
                used[j] = True
                found = True
                break
            k += 1

    if not found:
        # opposite parity
        if i_parity == 1:
            # odd -> even
            k = ptr_e
            while k < len(evens):
                j = evens[k]
                if not used[j] and math.gcd(i, j) > 1:
                    pairs.append((i, j))
                    used[j] = True
                    found = True
                    break
                k += 1
        else:
            # even -> odd
            k = ptr_o
            while k < len(odds):
                j = odds[k]
                if not used[j] and math.gcd(i, j) > 1:
                    pairs.append((i, j))
                    used[j] = True
                    found = True
                    break
                k += 1

print(len(pairs))
for a, b in pairs:
    print(a, b)

```python
import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(100000)

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
k = int(data[index])
index += 1

park_label = [[0] * n for _ in range(4)]
for i in range(4):
    for j in range(n):
        park_label[i][j] = int(data[index])
        index += 1

current_grid = [[0] * n for _ in range(4)]
for j in range(n):
    current_grid[1][j] = park_label[1][j]
    current_grid[2][j] = park_label[2][j]

park_target = {}
home = [None] * (k + 1)
car_pos = [None] * (k + 1)

for r in [0, 3]:
    for c in range(n):
        x = park_label[r][c]
        if x > 0:
            park_target[x] = (r, c)

for r in [1, 2]:
    for c in range(n):
        x = current_grid[r][c]
        if x > 0:
            car_pos[x] = (r, c)

for x in range(1, k + 1):
    tr, tc = park_target[x]
    hr = 1 if tr == 0 else 2
    home[x] = (hr, tc)

def is_parked(x):
    if x not in park_target:
        return True
    tr, tc = park_target[x]
    return current_grid[tr][tc] == x

def all_parked():
    for x in range(1, k + 1):
        if not is_parked(x):
            return False
    return True

def count_lane_cars():
    cnt = 0
    for r in [1, 2]:
        for c in range(n):
            if current_grid[r][c] > 0:
                cnt += 1
    return cnt

def compute_dists():
    row_d = 0
    col_d = 0
    for x in range(1, k + 1):
        if is_parked(x):
            continue
        cr, cc = car_pos[x]
        hr, hc = home[x]
        row_d += abs(cr - hr)
        col_d += abs(cc - hc)
    return row_d, col_d

moves = []
current_row_dist, current_col_dist = compute_dists()

while len(moves) <= 20000 and not all_parked():
    parked_some = False
    # Park all ready cars
    for c in range(n):
        for lane_r, park_r in [(1, 0), (2, 3)]:
            x = current_grid[lane_r][c]
            if x > 0 and park_target.get(x) == (park_r, c):
                # Park it
                moves.append((x, park_r + 1, c + 1))
                current_grid[lane_r][c] = 0
                current_grid[park_r][c] = x
                car_pos[x] = (park_r, c)
                parked_some = True
    if parked_some:
        current_row_dist, current_col_dist = compute_dists()
        continue

    # Check if lanes full
    if count_lane_cars() == 2 * n:
        print(-1)
        sys.exit(0)

    # Greedy best move
    best_score = (float('inf'), float('inf'), float('inf'), float('inf'), float('inf'))
    best_move = None
    dirs = [(-1, 0), (1, 0), (0, -1), (0, 1)]
    dir_idx = {(-1,0):0, (1,0):1, (0,-1):2, (0,1):3}

    for r in range(4):
        for c in range(n):
            x = current_grid[r][c]
            if x == 0:
                continue
            cr, cc = r, c
            hr, hc = home[x]
            old_is_parked = (park_target.get(x) == (cr, cc))
            old_row_d = 0 if old_is_parked else abs(cr - hr)
            old_col_d = 0 if old_is_parked else abs(cc - hc)
            for dr, dc in dirs:
                nr = r + dr
                nc = c + dc
                if not (0 <= nr < 4 and 0 <= nc < n):
                    continue
                if current_grid[nr][nc] != 0:
                    continue
                if nr in (0, 3) and park_target.get(x) != (nr, nc):
                    continue
                # Legal
                new_is_parked = (park_target.get(x) == (nr, nc))
                new_row_d = 0 if new_is_parked else abs(nr - hr)
                new_col_d = 0 if new_is_parked else abs(nc - hc)
                if new_is_parked:
                    delta_row = -old_row_d
                    delta_col = -old_col_d
                else:
                    delta_row = new_row_d - old_row_d
                    delta_col = new_col_d - old_col_d
                new_row_total = current_row_dist + delta_row
                new_col_total = current_col_dist + delta_col
                new_total_dist = new_row_total + new_col_total
                score = (new_total_dist, new_col_total, new_row_total, x, dir_idx[(dr, dc)])
                if score < best_score:
                    best_score = score
                    best_move = (x, nr + 1, nc + 1, r, c)

    if best_move is None:
        print(-1)
        sys.exit(0)

    # Perform best move
    x, nr1, nc1, old_r, old_c = best_move
    nr = nr1 - 1
    nc = nc1 - 1
    current_grid[old_r][old_c] = 0
    current_grid[nr][nc] = x
    car_pos[x] = (nr, nc)
    moves.append((x, nr1, nc1))
    current_row_dist, current_col_dist = compute_dists()

if all_parked() and len(moves) <= 20000:
    print(len(moves))
    for move in moves:
        print(move[0], move[1], move[2])
else:
    print(-1)

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().strip()
n = len(data)
s = data

prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + (1 if s[i] == '|' else 0)

has_open_before = [False] * (n + 1)
for i in range(n):
    has_open_before[i + 1] = has_open_before[i] or (s[i] == '[')

has_close_after = [False] * n
if n > 0:
    has_close_after[n - 1] = (s[n - 1] == ']')
for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
    has_close_after[i] = has_close_after[i + 1] or (s[i + 1] == ']')

min_prev = float('inf')
max_len = -1
seen_valid_p2 = False

for i in range(n):
    if s[i] == ':' and (i < n and has_close_after[i]):
        if seen_valid_p2:
            diff = prefix[i] - min_prev
            max_len = max(max_len, diff + 4)
    if s[i] == ':' and has_open_before[i]:
        min_prev = min(min_prev, prefix[i])
        seen_valid_p2 = True

print(max_len if max_len != -1 else -1)

```python
import sys
import heapq

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

idx = 0
n = int(data[idx])
idx += 1
d = int(data[idx])
idx += 1

a = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(2, n):
    a[i] = int(data[idx])
    idx += 1

x = [0] * (n + 1)
y = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    x[i] = int(data[idx])
    idx += 1
    y[i] = int(data[idx])
    idx += 1

dist = [[0] * (n + 1) for _ in range(n + 1)]
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    for j in range(1, n + 1):
        if i != j:
            dist[i][j] = abs(x[i] - x[j]) + abs(y[i] - y[j])

INF = 10**18

def check(M):
    max_net = [-INF] * (n + 1)
    max_net[1] = 0
    pq = []
    heapq.heappush(pq, (0, 1))  # (-net, u)
    while pq:
        negn, u = heapq.heappop(pq)
        net = -negn
        if net < max_net[u]:
            continue
        for v in range(1, n + 1):
            if v == u:
                continue
            dd = dist[u][v]
            cost = d * dd
            thresh = cost - M
            if net < thresh:
                continue
            new_net = net + a[v] - cost
            if new_net > max_net[v]:
                max_net[v] = new_net
                heapq.heappush(pq, (-new_net, v))
    return max_net[n] != -INF

low = 0
high = 10**8
while low < high:
    mid = (low + high) // 2
    if check(mid):
        high = mid
    else:
        low = mid + 1

print(low)

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
d = int(data[index])
index += 1
m = int(data[index])
index += 1

a = []
for i in range(n):
    a.append(int(data[index]))
    index += 1

safes = []
dangs = []
for x in a:
    if x <= m:
        safes.append(x)
    else:
        dangs.append(x)

D = len(dangs)
ns = len(safes)

safes.sort()
dangs.sort()

prefix_s = [0] * (ns + 1)
for i in range(1, ns + 1):
    prefix_s[i] = prefix_s[i - 1] + safes[i - 1]

prefix_d = [0] * (D + 1)
for i in range(1, D + 1):
    prefix_d[i] = prefix_d[i - 1] + dangs[i - 1]

total = sum(a)

max_k = 1 + (n - 1) // (d + 1)

ans = 0

# Handle k=0
if D == 0:
    ans = total

# Handle k >= 1
for k in range(1, min(D, max_k) + 1):
    w_min_cover = (k - 1) * d
    need_hide = D - k
    w = max(w_min_cover, need_hide)
    if w > n - k:
        continue
    num_w_safe = w - need_hide
    if num_w_safe > ns:
        continue
    wasted = prefix_d[need_hide] + prefix_s[num_w_safe]
    spoken = total - wasted
    if spoken > ans:
        ans = spoken

print(ans)

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
d = int(data[index])
index += 1
m = int(data[index])
index += 1

a = []
for i in range(n):
    a.append(int(data[index]))
    index += 1

safes = []
dangs = []
for x in a:
    if x <= m:
        safes.append(x)
    else:
        dangs.append(x)

D = len(dangs)
ns = len(safes)

safes.sort()
dangs.sort()

prefix_s = [0] * (ns + 1)
for i in range(1, ns + 1):
    prefix_s[i] = prefix_s[i - 1] + safes[i - 1]

prefix_d = [0] * (D + 1)
for i in range(1, D + 1):
    prefix_d[i] = prefix_d[i - 1] + dangs[i - 1]

total = sum(a)

max_k = 1 + (n - 1) // (d + 1)

ans = 0

# Handle k=0
if D == 0:
    ans = total

# Handle k >= 1
for k in range(1, min(D, max_k) + 1):
    w_min_cover = (k - 1) * d
    need_hide = D - k
    w = max(w_min_cover, need_hide)
    if w > n - k:
        continue
    num_w_safe = w - need_hide
    if num_w_safe > ns:
        continue
    wasted = prefix_d[need_hide] + prefix_s[num_w_safe]
    spoken = total - wasted
    if spoken > ans:
        ans = spoken

print(ans)
```

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
T = int(data[index])
index += 1

Q = [[] for _ in range(T + 1)]
for i in range(n):
    t = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    q = int(data[index])
    index += 1
    h = T - t
    Q[h].append(q)

MAX_D = T
MAX_S = 1025

prefix = [[] for _ in range(MAX_D + 1)]
for d in range(MAX_D + 1):
    Q[d].sort(reverse=True)
    pref = [0]
    for val in Q[d]:
        pref.append(pref[-1] + val)
    prefix[d] = pref

dp = [[0] * (MAX_S + 1) for _ in range(MAX_D + 2)]

for d in range(MAX_D, -1, -1):
    sz = len(prefix[d]) - 1
    ps = prefix[d]
    for s in range(MAX_S + 1):
        best = 0
        max_m = min(s, sz)
        for m in range(max_m + 1):
            next_s_raw = 2 * (s - m)
            next_s = min(MAX_S, next_s_raw)
            val = ps[m] + dp[d + 1][next_s]
            if val > best:
                best = val
        dp[d][s] = best

print(dp[0][1])
