```python
import sys
import math

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
n = int(data[0])
idx = 1
vectors = []
for i in range(n):
    x = int(data[idx])
    y = int(data[idx + 1])
    vectors.append((x, y, i))
    idx += 2

# Sort by decreasing magnitude squared, then by increasing atan2
sorted_vectors = sorted(vectors, key=lambda v: (-(v[0] ** 2 + v[1] ** 2), math.atan2(v[1], v[0])))

px = 0
py = 0
signs = [0] * n
for x, y, i in sorted_vectors:
    dot = px * x + py * y
    if dot > 0:
        signs[i] = -1
        px -= x
        py -= y
    else:
        signs[i] = 1
        px += x
        py += y

print(' '.join(map(str, signs)))

for i in range(n + 1):
    span_x = a[i + n - 1] - a[i]
    if i == 0:
        min_y = a[n]
        max_y = a[N - 1]
    elif i == n:
        min_y = a[0]
        max_y = a[n - 1]
    else:
        min_y = a[0]
        max_y = a[N - 1]
    span_y = max_y - min_y
    area = span_x * span_y
    if area < min_area:
        min_area = area

import sys
from collections import Counter

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index]); index += 1
m = int(data[index]); index += 1
k = int(data[index]); index += 1

alice = [int(data[index + i]) for i in range(n)]
index += n
bob = [int(data[index + i]) for i in range(m)]

cntA = Counter(alice)
cntB = Counter(bob)

types = sorted(set(alice) | set(bob))

suf = 0
possible = False
for i in range(len(types) - 1, -1, -1):
    t = types[i]
    da = cntA[t]
    db = cntB[t]
    suf += da - db
    if suf > 0:
        possible = True
        break

print("YES" if possible else "NO")

```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

typedef long long ll;
const ll INF = 4e18;

struct UF {
    vector<int> par;
    UF(int n) : par(n + 1) {
        for (int i = 1; i <= n; ++i) par[i] = i;
    }
    int find(int x) {
        return par[x] == x ? x : par[x] = find(par[x]);
    }
    void uni(int x, int y) {
        x = find(x);
        y = find(y);
        if (x != y) par[x] = y;
    }
};

int main() {
    int N, M;
    ll A, B;
    cin >> N >> M >> A >> B;
    vector<tuple<int, int, ll>> roads(M);
    vector<vector<int>> adj_a(N + 1);
    for (int i = 0; i
```python
import sys
input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index]); index += 1
m = int(data[index]); index += 1
a = int(data[index]); index += 1
b = int(data[index]); index += 1

roads = []
for _ in range(m):
    u = int(data[index]); index += 1
    v = int(data[index]); index += 1
    c = int(data[index]); index += 1
    roads.append((u, v, c))

class UF:
    def __init__(self, n):
        self.par = list(range(n + 1))

    def find(self, x):
        if self.par[x] != x:
            self.par[x] = self.find(self.par[x])
        return self.par[x]

    def uni(self, x, y):
        px = self.find(x)
        py = self.find(y)
        if px != py:
            self.par[px] = py

uf = UF(n)
for u, v, c in roads:
    if c == a:
        uf.uni(u, v)

comp = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    comp[i] = uf.find(i)

INF = 4 * 10**18
dist_a = [[INF] * (n + 1) for _ in range(n + 1)]
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    dist_a[i][i] = 0
for u, v, c in roads:
    if c == a:
        dist_a[u][v] = a
        dist_a[v][u] = a

for k in range(1, n + 1):
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        for j in range(1, n + 1):
            if dist_a[i][k] < INF and dist_a[k][j] < INF:
                dist_a[i][j] = min(dist_a[i][j], dist_a[i][k] + dist_a[k][j])

b_list = []
for u, v, c in roads:
    if c == b:
        b_list.append((u, v))
        b_list.append((v, u))
Mb = len(b_list)

meta = [[] for _ in range(Mb + 1)]
S = Mb
for i in range(Mb):
    uu, vv = b_list[i]
    if comp[uu] == comp[1] and dist_a[1][uu] < INF:
        cost = dist_a[1][uu] + b
        meta[S].append((i, cost))

for i in range(Mb):
    uu, vv = b_list[i]
    for j in range(Mb):
        u2, v2 = b_list[j]
        if comp[vv] == comp[u2] and dist_a[vv][u2] < INF:
            cost = dist_a[vv][u2] + b
            meta[i].append((j, cost))

import heapq
d = [INF] * (Mb + 1)
d[S] = 0
pq = []
heapq.heappush(pq, (0, S))
while pq:
    cost, x = heapq.heappop(pq)
    if cost > d[x]:
        continue
    for y, w in meta[x]:
        nc = cost + w
        if nc < d[y]:
            d[y] = nc
            heapq.heappush(pq, (nc, y))

ans = [INF] * (n + 1)
for p in range(1, n + 1):
    if dist_a[1][p] < INF:
        ans[p] = dist_a[1][p]

for p in range(1, n + 1):
    if comp[1] == comp[p]:
        continue
    for i in range(Mb):
        uu, vv = b_list[i]
        if comp[vv] == comp[p] and dist_a[vv][p] < INF:
            ans[p] = min(ans[p], d[i] + dist_a[vv][p])

print(' '.join(map(str, ans[1:n+1])))

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().splitlines()

n = int(data[0])
words = data[1:1+n]

def normalize(s):
    t = s
    while 'kh' in t:
        t = t.replace('kh', 'h')
    result = []
    i = 0
    while i < len(t):
        if t[i] in ('o', 'u'):
            j = i
            count_u = 0
            while j < len(t) and t[j] in ('o', 'u'):
                if t[j] == 'u':
                    count_u += 1
                j += 1
            count_o = j - i - count_u
            w = count_o + 2 * count_u
            result.append(f"U{str(w).zfill(2)}")
            i = j
        else:
            result.append(t[i])
            i += 1
    return ''.join(result)

unique = set()
for word in words:
    norm = normalize(word)
    unique.add(norm)

print(len(unique))
```

completed 137/150, Solved: True, number of success = 46/137, acc = 33.58
```python
import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(10**6)

def max_lucky(s, lo, hi):
    if hi - lo + 1 < 2:
        return 0
    # Find position of maximum
    p = lo
    for i in range(lo + 1, hi + 1):
        if s[i] > s[p]:
            p = i
    M = s[p]
    left_max = max_lucky(s, lo, p - 1)
    right_max = max_lucky(s, p + 1, hi)
    # Crossing: suffix maxima left and prefix maxima right
    cross = 0
    # Left suffix maxima
    cur_max = -1
    for j in range(p - 1, lo - 1, -1):
        if s[j] > cur_max:
            cross = max(cross, M ^ s[j])
            cur_max = s[j]
    # Right prefix maxima
    cur_max = -1
    for j in range(p + 1, hi + 1):
        if s[j] > cur_max:
            cross = max(cross, M ^ s[j])
            cur_max = s[j]
    return max(left_max, right_max, cross)

n = int(input())
s = list(map(int, input().split()))
ans = max_lucky(s, 0, n - 1)
print(ans)
```
```python
import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(10**6)

def main():
    n = int(input())
    s = list(map(int, input().split()))
    lchild = [-1] * n
    rchild = [-1] * n
    stack = []
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        last = -1
        while stack and s[stack[-1]] <= s[i]:
            last = stack.pop()
        lchild[i] = last
        if stack:
            rchild[stack[-1]] = i
        else:
            root = i
        stack.append(i)

    def max_lucky(rt):
        if rt == -1:
            return 0
        lm = max_lucky(lchild[rt])
        rm = max_lucky(rchild[rt])
        M = s[rt]
        cross = 0
        # left suffix maxima: right spine of left child
        cur = lchild[rt]
        while cur != -1:
            cross = max(cross, M ^ s[cur])
            cur = rchild[cur]
        # right prefix maxima: left spine of right child
        cur = rchild[rt]
        while cur != -1:
            cross = max(cross, M ^ s[cur])
            cur = lchild[cur]
        return max(lm, rm, cross)

    ans = max_lucky(root)
    print(ans)

main()
```
completed 138/150, Solved: True, number of success = 47/138, acc = 34.06
```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
using ll = long long;

const int M = 200010;
const int INF = 1e9 + 10;
vector<int> spf(M);

struct Info {
    int min1 = INF;
    int min2 = INF;
    int cnt = 0;
};

void sieve() {
    for (int i = 0; i < M; i++) spf[i] = i;
    spf[1] = 1;
    for (long long i = 2; i < M; i++) {
        if (spf[i] == i) {
            for (long long j = i * i; j < M; j += i) {
                if (spf[j] == j) spf[j] = i;
            }
        }
    }
}

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(0);
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<int> a(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> a[i];
    }
    sieve();
    map<int, Info> prime_info;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        int x = a[i];
        if (x == 1) continue;
        while (x > 1) {
            int p = spf[x];
            int e = 0;
            while (x % p == 0) {
                x /= p;
                e++;
            }
            Info& inf = prime_info[p];
            inf.cnt++;
            if (e < inf.min1) {
                inf.min2 = inf.min1;
                inf.min1 = e;
            } else if (e < inf.min2) {
                inf.min2 = e;
            }
        }
    }
    ll ans = 1;
    for (const auto& pr : prime_info) {
        int p = pr.first;
        const Info& inf = pr.second;
        int k = inf.cnt;
        int cnt0 = n - k;
        int ee = 0;
        if (cnt0 == 0) {
            ee = inf.min2;
        } else if (cnt0 == 1) {
            ee = inf.min1;
        }
        if (ee > 0) {
            ll contrib = 1;
            for (int j = 0; j < ee; j++) {
                contrib *= p;
            }
            ans *= contrib;
        }
    }
    cout << ans << '\n';
}
```
```python
import sys

M = 200010
INF = 10**9 + 10
spf = [0] * M

def sieve():
    for i in range(M):
        spf[i] = i
    spf[1] = 1
    for i in range(2, M):
        if spf[i] == i:
            j = i * i
            while j < M:
                if spf[j] == j:
                    spf[j] = i
                j += i

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()
index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
a = [int(data[index + i]) for i in range(n)]
index += n

sieve()
prime_info = {}
for x in a:
    if x == 1:
        continue
    cur_x = x
    while cur_x > 1:
        p = spf[cur_x]
        e = 0
        while cur_x % p == 0:
            cur_x //= p
            e += 1
        if p not in prime_info:
            prime_info[p] = {'min1': INF, 'min2': INF, 'cnt': 0}
        inf = prime_info[p]
        inf['cnt'] += 1
        if e < inf['min1']:
            inf['min2'] = inf['min1']
            inf['min1'] = e
        elif e < inf['min2']:
            inf['min2'] = e

ans = 1
for p, inf in prime_info.items():
    k = inf['cnt']
    cnt0 = n - k
    ee = 0
    if cnt0 == 0:
        ee = inf['min2']
    elif cnt0 == 1:
        ee = inf['min1']
    if ee > 0:
        contrib = p ** ee
        ans *= contrib

print(ans)

        b2 = n + 1 - j2

        p[b1] = b2
        p[b2] = a1
    print(' '.join(map(str, p[1:n+1])))

if n % 4 == 2 or n % 4 == 3:
    print(-1)
else:
    p = [0] * (n + 1)
    if n % 2 == 1:
        m = (n + 1) // 2
        p[m] = m
    num_pairs = n // 2
    for grp in range(num_pairs // 2):
        j1 = 2 * grp + 1
        j2 = j1 + 1
        a1 = j1
        b1 = n + 1 - j1
        a2 = j2
        b2 = n + 1 - j2
        p[a1] = a2
        p[a2] = b1
        p[b1] = b2
        p[b2] = a1
    print(' '.join(map(str, p[1:n+1])))
```

```cpp
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(nullptr);
    cout << fixed << setprecision(10);

    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<vector<int>> adj(n + 1);
    for (int i = 0; i < n - 1; ++i) {
        int u, v;
        cin >> u >> v;
        adj[u].push_back(v);
        adj[v].push_back(u);
    }

    vector<double> probs(n + 1);
    for (int root = 1; root <= n; ++root) {
        vector<vector<int>> child(n + 1);
        function<void(int, int)> build_tree = [&](int u, int p) {
            for (int v : adj[u]) {
                if (v != p) {
                    child[u].push_back(v);
                    build_tree(v, u);
                }
            }
        };
        build_tree(root, -1);

        function<double(int)> compute_g = [&](int u) -> double {
            vector<double> gs;
            for (int c : child[u]) {
                gs.push_back(compute_g(c));
            }
            vector<double> poly = {1.0};
            for (double gv : gs) {
                double a = gv;
                double b = 1.0 - gv;
                size_t sz = poly.size();
                vector<double> np(sz + 1, 0.0);
                for (size_t i = 0; i < sz; ++i) {
                    np[i] += a * poly[i];
                    np[i + 1] += b * poly[i];
                }
                poly = std::move(np);
            }
            double integ = 0.0;
            for (size_t k = 0; k < poly.size(); ++k) {
                integ += poly[k] / (k + 1.0);
            }
            return 0.5 * integ;
        };

        double p = 1.0;
        for (int c : child[root]) {
            p *= compute_g(c);
        }
        probs[root] = p;
    }

    for (int i = 1; i <= n; ++i) {
        cout << probs[i] << '\n';
    }
    return 0;
}
```

## Explanation

The provided code solves the problem of computing the probability that each vertex label survives the random edge contraction process in a tree. The probabilities are derived using dynamic programming on rooted trees, leveraging the uniform randomness of edge contraction orders.

Key insights:
- For a tree rooted at vertex \( r \), the survival probability \( p_r \) is the product of \( g(c) \) over all direct children \( c \) of \( r \), where \( g(u) \) is the expected contribution \( 2^{-m_{\text{branch}}(u)} \) for a parent absorbing subtree \( T_u \).
- \( g(u) = \frac{1}{2} \int_0^1 \prod_{c \in \text{children of } u} \bigl( g(c) + t (1 - g(c)) \bigr) \, dt \), computed exactly via polynomial multiplication and integration of coefficients.
- Leaves have \( g = 0.5 \) (parent pays \( \frac{1}{2} \), adds no subtrees).

Algorithm:
1. Build adjacency list from edges.
2. For each root \( r = 1 \) to \( n \):
   - DFS from \( r \) to construct children lists for the rooted tree.
   - Recursive function `compute_g(u)`:
     - Compute \( g(c) \) for each child \( c \) of \( u \).
     - Initialize polynomial \( p(t) = 1 \).
     - For each child, multiply \( p(t) \) by linear \( g(c) + t(1 - g(c)) \) using coefficient updates.
     - Integrate: \( \int_0^1 p(t) \, dt = \sum_k \frac{\text{coeff}_k}{k+1} \).
     - Return \( g(u) = 0.5 \times \text{integral} \).
   - Compute \( p_r = \prod_{c \in \text{children of } r} g(c) \) (empty product = 1 for leaves).
3. Output \( p_1 \) to \( p_n \) with 10 decimal places.

Time complexity: \( O(n^3) \) worst-case (50 rootings, each \( O(n^2) \) for polynomial operations), efficient for \( n \leq 50 \).

This matches samples: e.g., star tree yields \( p_1 = 0.125 \), \( p_{2,3,4} \approx 0.2917 \).
```python
import sys

sys.setrecursionlimit(10000)

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

idx = 0
n = int(data[idx])
idx += 1

adj = [[] for _ in range(n + 1)]
for _ in range(n - 1):
    u = int(data[idx])
    idx += 1
    v = int(data[idx])
    idx += 1
    adj[u].append(v)
    adj[v].append(u)

probs = [0.0] * (n + 1)

for root in range(1, n + 1):
    child = [[] for _ in range(n + 1)]

    def build_tree(u, p):
        for v in adj[u]:
            if v != p:
                child[u].append(v)
                build_tree(v, u)

    build_tree(root, 0)

    def compute_g(u):
        gs = [compute_g(c) for c in child[u]]
        poly = [1.0]
        for gv in gs:
            a = gv
            b = 1.0 - gv
            sz = len(poly)
            np = [0.0] * (sz + 1)
            for i in range(sz):
                np[i] += a * poly[i]
                np[i + 1] += b * poly[i]
            poly = np
        integ = 0.0
        for k in range(len(poly)):
            integ += poly[k] / (k + 1)
        return 0.5 * integ

    p = 1.0
    for c in child[root]:
        p *= compute_g(c)
    probs[root] = p

for i in range(1, n + 1):
    print(f"{probs[i]:.10f}")
```

```python
import sys
import bisect

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

n = int(data[0])
beacons = []
index = 1
for i in range(n):
    a = int(data[index])
    b = int(data[index + 1])
    beacons.append((a, b))
    index += 2

beacons.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])

pos = [0] * (n + 1)
power = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    pos[i] = beacons[i - 1][0]
    power[i] = beacons[i - 1][1]

reach = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    target = pos[i] - power[i]
    j = bisect.bisect_left(pos, target, lo=1, hi=i + 1)
    reach[i] = j

S = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    nxt = reach[i] - 1
    S[i] = 1 + (S[nxt] if nxt >= 1 else 0)

maxS = max(S)
ans = n - maxS
print(ans)
```

power = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    pos[i] = beacons[i - 1][0]
    power[i] = beacons[i - 1][1]

for i in range(1, n + 1):
    target = pos[i] - power[i]
    j = bisect.bisect_left(pos, target, lo=1, hi=i + 1)
    reach[i] = j

for i in range(1, n + 1):
    nxt = reach[i] - 1
    S[i] = 1 + (S[nxt] if nxt >= 1 else 0)

print(ans)

```python
import sys

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
n = int(data[0])
a = data[1]
b = data[2]

p = 0
q = 0
savings = 0
i = 0
while i < n:
    if a[i] == b[i]:
        i += 1
        continue
    # mismatch
    run_len = 1
    is_extra = (a[i] == '1')
    if is_extra:
        p += 1
    else:
        q += 1
    j = i + 1
    while j < n and a[j] != b[j]:
        next_extra = (a[j] == '1')
        if next_extra == is_extra:
            break
        run_len += 1
        if next_extra:
            p += 1
        else:
            q += 1
        is_extra = next_extra
        j += 1
    savings += run_len // 2
    i = j

cost = p + q - savings
print(cost)

```python
import sys
import bisect

INF = 10**18 + 5

def build_segtree(n):
    N = n + 1
    sz = 1
    while sz < N:
        sz <<= 1
    tree = [INF] * (2 * sz)
    return tree, sz

def update(tree, sz, pos, val):
    pos += sz
    tree[pos] = val
    pos >>= 1
    while pos >= 1:
        tree[pos] = min(tree[2 * pos], tree[2 * pos + 1])
        pos >>= 1

def query(tree, sz, L, R):
    res = INF
    L += sz
    R += sz
    while L <= R:
        if L & 1:
            res = min(res, tree[L])
            L += 1
        if not (R & 1):
            res = min(res, tree[R])
            R -= 1
        L >>= 1
        R >>= 1
    return res

def can(v, n, k, D):
    tree, sz = build_segtree(n)
    update(tree, sz, 0, 0)
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        target = v[i - 1] - D
        L = bisect.bisect_left(v, target)
        R = i - k
        if R < 0 or L > R:
            continue
        min_prev = query(tree, sz, L, R)
        if min_prev == INF:
            continue
        update(tree, sz, i, min_prev + 1)
    return query(tree, sz, n, n) != INF

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
k = int(data[index])
index += 1
v = [int(x) for x in data[index:index + n]]
v.sort()

low = 0
high = 10**9 + 1
while low < high:
    mid = (low + high) // 2
    if can(v, n, k, mid):
        high = mid
    else:
        low = mid + 1
print(low)
```
```python
import sys
import bisect

INF = 10**18 + 5

def build_segtree(n):
    N = n + 1
    sz = 1
    while sz < N:
        sz <<= 1
    tree = [INF] * (2 * sz)
    return tree, sz

def update(tree, sz, pos, val):
    pos += sz
    tree[pos] = val
    pos >>= 1
    while pos >= 1:
        tree[pos] = min(tree[2 * pos], tree[2 * pos + 1])
        pos >>= 1

def query(tree, sz, L, R):
    res = INF
    L += sz
    R += sz
    while L <= R:
        if L & 1:
            res = min(res, tree[L])
            L += 1
        if not (R & 1):
            res = min(res, tree[R])
            R -= 1
        L >>= 1
        R >>= 1
    return res

def can(v, n, k, D):
    tree, sz = build_segtree(n)
    update(tree, sz, 0, 0)
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        target = v[i - 1] - D
        L = bisect.bisect_left(v, target)
        R = i - k
        if R < 0 or L > R:
            continue
        min_prev = query(tree, sz, L, R)
        if min_prev == INF:
            continue
        update(tree, sz, i, min_prev + 1)
    return query(tree, sz, n, n) != INF

data = sys.stdin.read().split()
index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
k = int(data[index])
index += 1
v = [int(x) for x in data[index:index + n]]
v.sort()

low = 0
high = 10**9 + 1
while low < high:
    mid = (low + high) // 2
    if can(v, n, k, mid):
        high = mid
    else:
        low = mid + 1
print(low)

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
l = int(data[index])
index += 1
r = int(data[index])
index += 1
Ql = int(data[index])
index += 1
Qr = int(data[index])
index += 1

w = []
for i in range(n):
    w.append(int(data[index]))
    index += 1

pref = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    pref[i] = pref[i - 1] + w[i - 1]

min_total = float('inf')
for k in range(n + 1):
    left_sum = pref[k]
    right_sum = pref[n] - pref[k]
    fixed = left_sum * l + right_sum * r
    leftc = k
    rightc = n - k
    pen = 0
    if leftc > rightc:
        pen = Ql * max(0, leftc - rightc - 1)
    elif rightc > leftc:
        pen = Qr * max(0, rightc - leftc - 1)
    total = fixed + pen
    if total < min_total:
        min_total = total

print(int(min_total))

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
l = int(data[index])
index += 1
r = int(data[index])
index += 1
Ql = int(data[index])
index += 1
Qr = int(data[index])
index += 1

w = []
for i in range(n):
    w.append(int(data[index]))
    index += 1

pref = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    pref[i] = pref[i - 1] + w[i - 1]

min_total = float('inf')
for k in range(n + 1):
    left_sum = pref[k]
    right_sum = pref[n] - pref[k]
    fixed_cost = left_sum * l + right_sum * r
    a = k
    b = n - k
    candidates = []
    sl_min = 1 if a > 0 else 0
    sr_min = 1 if b > 0 else 0
    # equal
    t = min(a, b)
    if t >= sl_min and t >= sr_min:
        candidates.append(Ql * t + Qr * t)
    # L more: sl = sr + 1
    if a > 0:
        t = min(b, a - 1)
        sl_ = t + 1
        sr_ = t
        if sl_ >= sl_min and sr_ >= sr_min:
            candidates.append(Ql * sl_ + Qr * sr_)
    # R more: sr = sl + 1
    if b > 0:
        t = min(a, b - 1)
        sl_ = t
        sr_ = t + 1
        if sl_ >= sl_min and sr_ >= sr_min:
            candidates.append(Ql * sl_ + Qr * sr_)
    maxw = max(candidates) if candidates else 0
    penalty = Ql * a + Qr * b - maxw
    total = fixed_cost + penalty
    if total < min_total:
        min_total = total

print(int(min_total))

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
k = int(data[index])
index += 1

c = [0] * (k + 1)
n = 0
for i in range(1, k + 1):
    c[i] = int(data[index])
    n += c[i]
    index += 1

MOD = 1000000007
MAXN = 1005
fact = [1] * MAXN
for i in range(1, MAXN):
    fact[i] = fact[i - 1] * i % MOD

invfact = [0] * MAXN
invfact[MAXN - 1] = pow(fact[MAXN - 1], MOD - 2, MOD)
for i in range(MAXN - 2, -1, -1):
    invfact[i] = invfact[i + 1] * (i + 1) % MOD

inv = [0] * MAXN
for i in range(1, MAXN):
    inv[i] = invfact[i] * fact[i - 1] % MOD

s = [0] * (k + 1)
for i in range(1, k + 1):
    s[i] = s[i - 1] + c[i]

res = fact[n]
for i in range(1, k + 1):
    res = res * invfact[c[i]] % MOD

prod_cs = 1
for i in range(1, k + 1):
    prod_cs = (prod_cs * c[i]) % MOD
res = res * prod_cs % MOD

for i in range(1, k + 1):
    res = res * inv[s[i]] % MOD

print(res)

```python
import sys

input = sys.stdin.read
data = input().split()

index = 0
n = int(data[index])
index += 1
k = int(data[index])
index += 1

a = []
for i in range(n):
    a.append(int(data[index]))
    index += 1

S = sum(a)
if S % k != 0:
    print("No")
    sys.exit(0)

T = S // k

prefix = [0] * (n + 1)
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    prefix[i] = prefix[i - 1] + a[i - 1]

sum_to_idx = {}
for i in range(1, n + 1):
    sum_to_idx[prefix[i]] = i

splits = []
current = 0
possible = True
for m in range(1, k):
    target = m * T
    if target not in sum_to_idx:
        possible = False
        break
    pos = sum_to_idx[target]
    splits.append(pos - current)
    current = pos

if not possible:
    print("No")
else:
    splits.append(n - current)
    print("Yes")
    print(' '.join(map(str, splits)))

```python
import sys
sys.setrecursionlimit(10000)

def get_cycles(n):
    if n == 3:
        return [[1, 2, 3], [1, 2, 3]]
    elif n == 4:
        return [[1, 2, 3], [1, 2, 4], [1, 3, 4], [2, 3, 4]]
    else:
        old = get_cycles(n - 2)
        new_c = []
        tri = [n - 1, n, 1]
        new_c += [tri, tri]
        A = list(range(2, n - 1))
        d = len(A)
        for i in range(d):
            p = A[i]
            q = A[(i + 1) % d]
            quad = [n - 1, p, n, q]
            new_c.append(quad)
        return old + new_c

n = int(input().strip())
cycles = get_cycles(n)
print(len(cycles))
for cyc in cycles:
    print(len(cyc), end=' ')
    for v in cyc:
        print(v, end=' ')
    print()
```
```python
import sys
sys.setrecursionlimit(10000)

def get_cycles(n):
    if n == 3:
        return [[1, 2, 3], [1, 2, 3]]
    elif n == 4:
        return [[1, 2, 3], [1, 2, 4], [1, 3, 4], [2, 3, 4]]
    else:
        old = get_cycles(n - 2)
        new_c = []
        tri = [n - 1, n, 1]
        new_c += [tri, tri]
        A = list(range(2, n - 1))
        d = len(A)
        for i in range(d):
            p = A[i]
            q = A[(i + 1) % d]
            quad = [n - 1, p, n, q]
            new_c.append(quad)
        return old + new_c

n = int(input().strip())
cycles = get_cycles(n)
print(len(cycles))
for cyc in cycles:
    print(len(cyc), end=' ')
    for v in cyc:
        print(v, end=' ')
    print()
